Gold and Silver 44

London Gold Price: The London gold price fell by five pence today, quoted at 141 shillings and eight pence.

London Silver Bars: The London silver market rose by 0.1875 today due to purchases by the US and Indian exchanges. The spot price is 23.9375 pence, and the futures price is 24.0625 pence. There were speculators buying and selling, and the market closed steadily.

Exchange Rates 45

British-American: The London foreign exchange market's pound sterling price remained stable against the US dollar. The opening exchange rate between the British pound and the US dollar was 4.93875, down 0.125. However, it quickly rose, gradually increasing in the morning. The most recent price at 2 p.m. was 4.95375, up 1.5 points from the opening. The pound's improvement was due to the replenishment of positions by European countries that were short on pounds. Also, one US dollar equals 4 shillings and 0.0448 pence in British gold.

British-French: The exchange rate between the British pound and the French franc also experienced changes, although the fluctuations were weaker. The opening price was 74.34 francs, down six points, but by 2 p.m., the price had risen by 0.31 francs to 74.65 francs.

American-British: The New York foreign exchange market saw little change in the US-British exchange rate this morning, except for a slight increase at the opening. The pound rose by 1.25 points at the opening, but there were no further changes. The most recent price was 4.95375, about 1.25 points higher than the opening.

Cotton and Wheat 46

American Cotton: The cotton market opened slightly higher, with little demand, but even fewer short sales. The market was quiet and inactive this morning.

British Cotton: The Liverpool cotton market was slightly better today. At 1 p.m., the December futures price was 6.67, up four points from yesterday's close.

British Wheat: The Liverpool wheat market plummeted this morning. The market was weak. At 1 p.m., the December futures price was 5 shillings and 1.625 pence, down 0.875.

American Wheat: The Chicago wheat market opened today, down 0.25 to 0.50, due to the very weak market in Liverpool and the current rainfall in the drought-stricken areas of the Southwest.

Rubber 47

London: The rubber market was quiet this morning, with a slight drop in the near term and no change in the far term. The trading price for the January-March period at noon was 7 pence, down 0.0625 from yesterday.

New York: The rubber market opened down 0.067 points, then rebounded slightly. The most recent price was about 0.03 points higher than the opening.

Wang Delin's Volunteer Army Once Occupied Xinlitun 50

(Tianjin) Over a thousand soldiers from Wang Delin's volunteer army appeared in the eastern forest area of Yushu County, Jilin Province, on the 15th of this month. They urgently dispatched Japanese and puppet troops from Shulan to reinforce. A fierce battle broke out on the night of the 16th, resulting in 60 Japanese soldiers killed and over a hundred puppet soldiers killed or wounded. Hebei Daming Tax Police Open Fire, Killing Salt Farmers in a Bloodbath 98

Death Toll Reaches as High as Thirty-Eight

Inspection Office Dispatches Personnel to Investigate the Truth

Tianjin Correspondence: The Eighth District Tax Office of the Changlu Salt Affairs Inspection Office, stationed in Daming, led by District Chief Yang Yi, dispatched police officers from the entire district to Zhao Gu Village in the county on the 8th of this month to destroy salt ponds. Local salt flat residents gathered to resist with weapons, leading to a conflict. Tax police opened fire on the spot, killing eighteen people and seriously injuring more than twenty. On the tax police side, one person went missing and seven were injured. After this incident occurred, the people of Daming County were quite agitated by the tax police's barbaric actions and the multiple deaths and injuries, creating a situation where the Eighth District tax police, who caused the incident, could not easily get away with it. The Changlu Salt Affairs Inspection Office considered the situation serious and specially dispatched Zhang Zhongli, Director of the Tax Police Bureau, to rush to the scene of the incident yesterday to investigate and find a solution nearby. The course of events is recorded as follows:

The sale of salt produced in the Changlu area has been sluggish recently. According to an investigation by the Salt Transportation Department, as many as seventy-three counties throughout Hebei Province are manufacturing and selling nitrate salt, affecting salt tax revenue and causing monthly losses. In recent months, only 1.8 million yuan has been collected each month. Changlu tax revenues are a source of military funding for the north, and 1.5 million yuan must be allocated to Beiping for military supplies each month. Zeng Yangfeng, the Salt Transportation Commissioner, in order to rectify the situation, first added tax police and dispatched Deputy Director Su of the Tax Police Bureau, along with tax police, to Gaoyang County, where the most nitrate salt is produced, for investigation. At the same time, a letter was sent to the Hebei Provincial Government requesting assistance in suppressing it. At 10:00 AM on the 8th of this month, the Daming Eighth District Tax Police, led by District Chief Yang Yi, went to the Zhao Gu Village nitrate salt ponds. The ponds were relied upon by hundreds of salt farmers as a source of food and clothing. Upon hearing that the tax police were coming, they gathered to resist and refused with armed force. Tax Police District Chief Yang Yi then ordered them to open fire. Initially, the one hundred and fifty tax police fired a volley into the air, intending to intimidate them, but the salt farmers did not retreat and instead charged forward. Yang then ordered them to fire a second time, killing eighteen people on the spot and seriously injuring more than twenty. The salt farmers, seeing deaths and injuries, retreated slightly. After the incident unfolded, Daming gentry and representatives of the salt farmers jointly appealed to the province, requesting that the Finance Ministry remove and punish District Chief Yang Yi, who caused the disaster by opening fire. Zeng Yangfeng, the Changlu Salt Transportation Commissioner, upon receiving the report, on the one hand ordered the tax police not to act rashly, and on the other hand requested the Provincial Government to telegraph Daming County Magistrate Cheng Tinghuan to properly appease and assist in resolving the matter. According to a telegram report received by the Provincial Government from Daming County Magistrate Cheng Tinghuan, the tax police opened fire for half an hour that day, consuming more than fifteen hundred rounds of ammunition. Salt farmers were lying dead and injured everywhere, in a very tragic state. Daming legal entities, at the request of the families of the injured and dead salt farmers, have sent telegrams to the Beiping Political Reorganization Committee and the Military Sub-Committee, demanding that the perpetrators be punished. According to the person in charge of the Changlu Salt Transportation Department, the Daming tax police destroying the salt ponds was done under orders. The Transportation Department stipulated a price of three jiao for every hundred catties of nitrate salt to be purchased in full, and forbade further violations. The measures were not inadequate, but the salt farmers resisted in reliance on their numbers, which was inappropriate. It was decided to handle it according to the law. As for the fact that the tax police, in the performance of their duties, opened fire and caused deaths, the department has also decided to handle it according to the law, it was said. (15th)

Henan, Hubei, and Anhui Border Area to be Designated a Special Administrative Region 99

Special Region Relief Association Submits to Henan Party Affairs Office

Kaifeng Correspondence: The Henan Special Region Relief Association, considering that the Henan, Hubei, and Anhui border area is mountainous and has suffered from banditry in the past, specially requested the Provincial Party Affairs Special Commissioner's Office yesterday to designate it as a special administrative region, in order to assign responsibility and eliminate the source of the chaos. The original submission from the association is recorded below: "Regarding the Henan, Hubei, and Anhui border area, with overlapping mountains and many bandits, we respectfully request that it be designated as a special administrative region in order to assign responsibility and eliminate the source of the chaos. We have investigated that the counties formerly under Ruguang in Henan are connected to Yingliu in the east and bordered by Huangma in the south. The myriad mountains intersect, and the streams and paths twist and turn, making every place a strategic point. Furthermore, they are far from the provincial capitals of each province, so if there is any trouble, it immediately becomes a situation beyond their reach. Therefore, those who plot wrongdoing seize the opportunity to cause disturbances. This can be seen throughout the Yuan and Ming dynasties. However, they were all bandit natures. Once defeated, they would flee elsewhere. Only the Red Bandits have ideology and organization. The local people, through their Red influence, are difficult to move. Over the years, although they have been repeatedly encircled and suppressed by large armies, and defeat has left them unable to form an army, the remaining bandit forces rise and fall intermittently, and there has been no way to settle the aftermath. Previously, Commissioner Chen Jicheng of the Ninth District of Henan suggested to the Central Government and the Ministry that a new province be established in the border area of the three provinces to unify military and civilian affairs. The Ministry of Interior approved, saying, "The establishment of a new province in the border area of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui is for the sake of pacifying the local area and facilitating administration. What has been stated is not without merit. The office should consider the local conditions and natural terrain in detail, make detailed plans, and submit three proposed province names, along with explanations of their meanings, to the ministry for further review and decision." Hearing this, we were greatly pleased, believing that once the special region was demarcated for governance, the displaced would surely return to their former occupations. However, this matter is of great importance, and the procedures are cumbersome, so it is feared that it cannot be realized in a short period of time. It is proposed that you consult the previous case submitted by Liu Zhenhua, the former commander of the three border regions for bandit suppression, and designate the counties formerly under Ruguang in Henan, the counties formerly under Yingliu in Anhui, Kongshan, Macheng, Luotian, Qishui, Huangmei in Hubei, as well as Shouchun, Fengtai, and other counties in Anhui, and set up more county governments in important places far from the county seats, to create a special administrative region in order to receive the effect of mutual assistance and to achieve the overall plan for complete elimination. In this way, the masses infected by Red influence will no longer be able to repeat their tricks of dividing the whole into parts and dividing the parts into wholes, avoiding the real and going to the virtual, making noise in the east and fleeing to the west. With no opportunity to seize, hidden dangers will naturally disappear. There is no better way to settle the aftermath than this. (17th)

Feng Yuxiang Arrives in Jinan 100

To Mourn His Old Friend Gu Liangyou

After Boarding the Train, He Sat Among the Poor

Feng Talks About His Recent Life Reading in the Mountains

Jinan Correspondence: Feng Yuxiang, who resides in Mount Tai, arrived quietly in Jinan this morning (the 17th) at 7:00 AM with light luggage and few attendants. It is reported that Mr. Feng received the shocking news last night (the 16th) that Gu Liangyou, Commander of the Third Route of the Shandong Militia, had passed away and was extremely saddened. He urgently wanted to come to Jinan to pay his respects in person. There were no trains heading north at that time, so he waited until about 3:00 AM this morning, in the dim starlight, and walked down the mountain. Those who came with him included the guard captain Wang Zhiyi, attendants Liu Chunde and Zu Mingfeng, and four guards. Liu Chunde and the others were initially unaware of where Feng was going when he left his residence late at night and were all worried and helpless, but they did not dare to stop him and simply followed. At 4:00 AM, they arrived at the Taian Railway Station. Two passenger trains were stopped at the station. Feng sent a follower to ask where the trains were going. After a short wait, the follower reported that the train was heading south. Feng was silent and unhappy. Soon after, another follower reported that the other train was heading north. Feng then urged them to buy eight third-class tickets. The attendants asked where to buy the tickets to, and Feng replied Jinan. At this point, Liu Chunde and the others realized that Feng was coming to Jinan to mourn a friend and were relieved. They then bought tickets and boarded the third-class passenger car. Feng sat precariously by the window in the car, while the attendants sat nearby to protect him secretly. When Feng first entered the car, most of the passengers in the car were poor people from southern Shandong going to the Northeast to make a living, supporting the old and carrying the young, wearing tattered clothes, in a very pitiful state. Seeing Feng arrive, they mostly looked at him strangely because of his height and build. An old farmer sat with Feng, nearly seventy years old. Feng looked at him and talked to him, asking where he was going. The old man replied that he was going to Tianjin to transfer to the Northeast to make a living. Feng then asked why he was leaving Guan to make a living. He replied that his family was very poor and it was difficult to make a living, so he had no choice but to leave his hometown and travel far to make a living outside the border. After talking for a long time, Feng took out the vernacular poems he had brought with him and gave them to the old man. The old man flipped through a few pages and fell asleep, while Feng read books by the window until dawn. When Feng arrived in Jinan and got off the train, the passengers in the car and the sleeping old farmer still did not know that this was Feng. Feng arrived in Jinan. Because no one knew about it in advance, no military or government officials came to the station to welcome him. Feng was still wearing a blue coarse cloth cotton trousers and jacket, black cloth cotton shoes, white cloth socks, and a coarse cloth cotton coat. After getting off the train, he walked out of the station and went straight to the municipal government. Someone who recognized Feng hurriedly reported to the municipal government by telephone. Mayor Wen Chenglie hurriedly went out to greet him and met him on the way. They went to the municipal government together to rest. At that time, provincial government advisors Ge Jinzhang and Guo Zhigang also heard the news and rushed to meet him. At around 8:00 AM, Feng, together with Wen Chenglie, Ge Jinzhang, Guo Zhigang, and others, went to Jinan Hospital to mourn Gu Liangyou. Feng saw the coffin and cried bitterly while stroking it. After much persuasion, he stopped crying and returned to the municipal government. At around 9:00 AM, Liu Xizhong, Director of the Provincial Automobile Road Bureau, Duan Yucun, Provincial Government Advisor, Zheng Jicheng, Provincial Government Counselor, and Chai Chunlin, Director of the Shandong Tax Police Bureau, successively visited Mr. Feng at the municipal government. Han Fuju, Chairman of the Provincial Government, was attending the Boy Scout Grand Camp outside the South Wuzimen Provincial Public Sports Field and did not arrive at the municipal government to meet Feng and have breakfast until 11:00 AM. At around 11:00 AM, after breakfast, Han returned to the provincial government, and Feng took a nap at the municipal government. At 11:30 AM, Feng boarded a special car prepared by Han and left Jinan to return to Tai.

Mr. Feng's Remarks 101

A reporter interviewed Mr. Feng at the municipal government, asking about his recent life and his thoughts on the current situation. According to Mr. Feng, "Yu and Gu Xinzhi (i.e., Gu Liangyou) were old friends for many years. After joining the army, we were together day and night, living together for more than ten years as if it were just one day, and we shared a bed for two years. Our friendship was closer than flesh and blood. Last night, I suddenly heard the shocking news and was overwhelmed with grief, so I rushed to Jinan today (the 17th) to pay my respects. I will not stay in Jinan and will return to Tai today. I will not attend the Fifth National Congress and have no thoughts on the current situation. Living in the mountains, reading and writing, I feel quite comfortable, so I have not been going elsewhere recently. In addition to continuing to work hard on poetry, books, rites, music, politics, economics, and social sciences, I often read new poetry in my spare time. The books I read in the car on the way from Tai to Jin today were selections of vernacular poems by Lu Xun, Hu Shi, Liu Bannong, Guo Moruo, and others. The spirit of new poetry can deeply describe the social state of the big bullying the small, the strong oppressing the weak, the rich suppressing the poor, and the disregard for women. As for the national spirit, national shame, and national humiliation, they should be sung with great emotion to inspire national pride. Among the poems of Shi, Bannong, and Moruo, Moruo's are the most powerful and can best represent the strong and unyielding blood of the Chinese nation. Zhao Wangyun, a rural photographer, previously created more than one hundred rural photographs, which nakedly depict rural life, the rural economy, and rural suffering and can well represent modern rural China. I wrote separate inscriptions on the photographs. Recently, Mr. Zhao traveled to the frontier, visiting Luowenyu, Gubeikou, Xifengkou, Zhangbeikou, and other places with anti-Japanese battle sites, and all were commemorated. He took photographs everywhere he went, compiling a total of one hundred and ten photographs. He previously sent them to me to write poems for them, and I have completed one hundred and six poems, with four still unfinished. I will complete them upon my return to the mountains tonight. In the past, Confucius wrote the Spring and Autumn Annals, and Zuo Qiuming wrote the Zuo Zhuan. Their brush strokes were critical, exposing the darkness of their time without reservation, making them the best historical records. Every time I read an article, if I felt something in my heart, I would write it down in a book. Over the years, I have collected more than one hundred articles, which I have now completed and will be published soon under the name "Reading the Spring and Autumn Annals and the Book of Rites." Recently, I have further organized my miscellaneous feelings from reading the Book of Documents and the Book of Poetry and am also preparing to compile them into a book under the name "Reading the Book of Documents, the Book of Poetry, and the Book of Rites." It will also be completed soon. I have decided to study and engage in writing in the future and will not ask about other matters. Many farmers in Taian raise silkworms, but they stick to the old methods and do not know how to improve them, so the results are not good. Previously, Mr. Cai Renbao wrote to me to discuss sending two people to Tai to provide guidance and asked me to select two farmers to go to Yidu to study silkworm breeding so that they could return to Tai to provide guidance. However, the farmers are all poor and it is difficult for them to leave home, so it did not happen. During my leisure time living in the mountains, I often walk in the mountains, look north with my head raised, and think of the four northeastern provinces that have fallen into the hands of foreigners, the beautiful rivers and mountains, the hundreds of cities, which have not yet been recovered. Tens of millions of compatriots, countless elders, brothers, aunts, and sisters, are all in deep water and fiery heat, crying and shouting, waiting for rescue. We who live in the interior, hoping and longing, cannot but be ashamed of ourselves. After the September 18th Incident, we relied on the League of Nations today and the League of Nations tomorrow. As of today, the League of Nations investigation team has long since returned east, and there is no solution. Furthermore, our country's seat on the League of Nations Council has been lost. The League of Nations' attitude towards China is clear. If the Chinese people do not rise up and struggle, it will be difficult to imagine the future. Batches of overseas Chinese residing in Japan are being deported back to the country, while the arrival of Asahi Shimbun airplanes in Tianjin is being celebrated on a grand scale. I wonder what the Chinese people think of this. As of today, the state of the nation is such that if the Chinese people do not wake up, unite sincerely, and resist foreign aggression together to overcome the difficulties of the time, there will be a danger of national subjugation. I sincerely hope that the whole country, from top to bottom, will understand this intention and rise up to save the country. There is still a glimmer of hope for the future of the nation," he said. (17th)

Northwest Inspection Report Special Correspondent of This Newspaper, Geng Ya

Gansu Province Education Situation 102

In recent years, education in Gansu Province has suffered from financial constraints, barely maintaining the status quo. Objectively, the number of schools has been increasing annually, but the facilities remain rudimentary. Few middle school graduates have the means to pursue further education, leading to a significant shortage of specialized talent. Furthermore, most county middle schools are headed by local gentry, resulting in uneven educational development across the counties.

In the provincial capital, school education is relatively developed. Higher education includes one Gansu College, divided into university and high school departments. The university department is further divided into four departments: law, medicine, literature, and agriculture, plus a special studies department. The high school department is divided into three levels. The total number of students in the college is over 250, with monthly expenses of 7,353,000 yuan. Secondary education includes the First Normal School, divided into higher and lower levels, with one normal class, six junior high classes, and eight attached elementary classes, totaling over 400 students (excluding the attached elementary school), with monthly expenses of 5,085,650 yuan. The First Middle School is divided into higher and lower levels, with six junior high classes and two senior high classes, totaling over 500 students, with monthly expenses of 4,739,800 yuan. The First Agricultural School has three general science classes, totaling over 160 students, with monthly expenses of 3,690,650 yuan. The Fifth Middle School has five junior high classes and six attached elementary classes, totaling over 140 students (excluding the attached elementary school), with monthly expenses of 2,511,970 yuan. The First Industrial School has three general science classes, totaling over 110 students, with monthly expenses of 3,690,650 yuan. The First Women's Normal School has one senior high normal class, four junior high classes, one kindergarten normal class, one vocational class, six attached elementary classes, and two kindergarten groups, totaling over 120 students (excluding the attached elementary school and kindergarten), with monthly expenses of 3,670,560 yuan.

The total monthly expenses for the above seven middle and high schools are 30,742.28 yuan. Divided among over 1,520 students, the monthly expense per student is over 20 yuan, excluding equipment costs. In addition to tuition and book fees, the total expense per middle and high school graduate over their years of study is over 1,400 yuan. If graduates have no avenues for engaging in social production after graduation, both society and the graduates will suffer adverse effects. Is this the true intention of education?

Educational administration in the province: (A) Higher education: changing domestic study fees to scholarships. In the past, the Education Department, aiming to cultivate specialized talent, set aside provincial-funded quotas at various domestic universities, colleges, and vocational schools. However, few provincial-funded students were able to enter national universities, while many entered private universities. Few were able to enter science and technology departments, while many entered social science departments, resulting in the education received not meeting the needs of the province. To correct this problem, the Education Department specifically changed domestic student fees to scholarships, providing provincial funding based on academic merit to increase learning efficiency. (B) Secondary education: issuing a general order for all secondary schools to add Tibetan language instruction and instructing the Fifth Middle School to establish special Mongolian-Tibetan classes. The Education Department previously received an order from the Ministry of Education approving the addition of Mongolian and Tibetan languages to the foreign language curriculum of secondary schools. Therefore, the Education Department, in addition to ordering the provincial Fifth Middle School to actively plan for the establishment of special Mongolian-Tibetan classes, also ordered all county-level middle schools to add Tibetan language instruction, using education as a means to develop the Northwest and promote culture. (C) Elementary education: the most important administrative task at present is to restore the closed elementary schools at all levels in the counties. Due to years of water and drought disasters, educational funding in the counties is on the verge of bankruptcy, resulting in the closure of many elementary schools at all levels. Elementary education is the foundation of all education, and rapid restoration is urgently needed. The current Education Department has already ordered the county education bureaus to strictly follow the restoration measures. (D) Social education: establishing public education centers and social education promotion offices. The establishment of public education centers requires enormous funding, so the Education Department plans to request the provincial government to transfer the Gansu Provincial Education Hall to the Education Department and convert it into a public education center. In addition, the Education Department has also established three social education promotion offices, each with propaganda, investigation, and sports divisions, with monthly expenses of 243 yuan. An additional 50 yuan per month has been added to establish reading rooms with books and newspapers. (E) Education funding: allocating all Gansu cigarette special taxes as education subsidies. The middle and high schools in the provincial capital require monthly expenses of over 30,000 yuan. The temporary maintenance meeting decided to allocate all income from the Gansu Transportation Bureau as special funds for these schools. After the reorganization and establishment of the provincial government, coinciding with the off-season, it was difficult to ensure sufficient special funds. Moreover, the county middle schools were owed a large amount, including arrears from the previous year and the first half of the 21st year. To maintain the current state of education in the province, the Education Department proposed to the provincial government to approve the allocation of income from the cigarette special tax bureau as education funding to assist. The Department also jointly formulated three measures with the Finance Department to guarantee this special education fund, which were approved and implemented by the provincial conference. As a result, Gansu's education funding, which had been relying on years of accumulated deficits, finally had reliable funds to maintain operations. If increased equipment funds are allocated to schools at all levels, regular expenses are reduced, and teacher salaries are increased, the future of education in Gansu will be promising.

Since taking office in the 21st year, the Director of the Education Department, Shui Chuqin, has strived to improve educational facilities to the best of his ability, even while maintaining the status quo. As a result, achievements have been made daily, and his reputation is quite good. It is said that Gansu Province has a complex ethnic composition, and the people have historically not valued reading. Before the founding of the Republic, the Hui and Tibetan ethnic groups absolutely prohibited their children from attending school. In recent years, Hui Muslim leaders have begun to advocate for education, but the number of Tibetan people who know how to read remains very small. The so-called development of the Northwest, whether in terms of water conservancy, transportation, farmland, mineral resources, or culture, cannot be achieved without first having detailed plans to seek equitable development. In terms of education, it is necessary to enrich and improve existing regular schools. However, without establishing special methods to educate and raise the cultural level of the majority of Hui and Tibetan compatriots, it is impossible to achieve the desired results. Fortunately, Hui and Tibetan leaders strongly support this, either by establishing separate Hui and Tibetan schools or by attaching special classes to various schools. However, due to continuous disasters and economic hardship in various regions, development and construction in any aspect cannot be effective without the strong support of the central government and people from the southeast.

In Gansu Province, the news media was only known to a few intellectuals around the end of the Guangxu era in the Qing Dynasty. After the founding of the Republic, the Kuomintang first published the Dahe Daily in Lanzhou. At the same time, the Republican Party also published the Lanzhou Daily, but both were subsequently discontinued. Between the fifth and sixth years of the Republic, the "Hesheng" and "Longyou Public Report" were published, but they were only fleeting. In the seventh year of the Republic, the Biansheng Weekly was published, aiming to harmonize the opinions of the Han and Hui ethnic groups, but it was discontinued after a year due to financial difficulties. In the fourteenth and fifteenth years, the National Revolutionary Army entered Gansu, and the Xinlong Daily and the Republic Daily, sponsored by the provincial party headquarters, were published. The Xinlong Daily was discontinued in the eighteenth year, but the Republic Daily continues to this day. Since the twentieth year, there has been a sudden surge in development, with newspapers and news agencies springing up like mushrooms after rain. There are four types of daily newspapers: Republic Daily, Northwest Daily, Xinlong Daily, and Longnan Minsheng Daily. There are two types of daily publications: Wuliang Voice and Wulan Daily. There are seven types of weekly publications: Huiguang Weekly, Bianguan Weekly, Longxi Minsheng, Hexi Weekly, Ganzhou Minsheng, Minyan Bao, and Heyang Weekly. There are twelve types of news agencies: Minjian News, Minyu News, Zhengwen News, Linxia News, Wuyang News, Hangdian News, Xingmin News, Jingtai News, Rural News, Xihe News, Sanlong News, and Bianwen News. In addition, there are publications from various agencies and schools, with numerous titles too numerous to list. However, they all make their respective contributions to social culture.

Songjiang County Chamber of Commerce Requests Revision of Stamp Tax Law 103

The County Chamber of Commerce believes that the stamp tax law compiled by the Legislative Yuan goes against commercial practices. Therefore, they telegraphed Sun Ke, President of the Legislative Yuan, requesting a revision. The message stated, in brief (greetings omitted): "Recently, we read in the newspaper that the stamp tax law only benefits those below three yuan, and those above three yuan are subject to progressive taxation, causing extreme harassment to merchants. Moreover, those who are not familiar with the law are at risk of being fined. At a time when rural areas are bankrupt and commerce is in decline, merchants are already unable to bear the burden. We urge the President to consider the difficulties of merchants, comply with public opinion, and approve revisions to alleviate the merchants' hardships."

Murder Case in a Thatched Shed in Wuxi 104

In a thatched shed near Xinglong Bridge outside the East Gate of Wuxi, near the Ye Qin Yarn Factory, lived Tang Kun, a 32-year-old Yixing native, who made a living by rowing Changzhou fast boats. His wife, Zhou, was somewhat attractive and worked as a female worker in the Ye Qin Yarn Factory. She recently became acquainted with Yuan Fuchang, a Taizhou native who worked as a leather craftsman nearby. Around 8 PM the previous night, Yuan sneaked into Tang's house again to rekindle their affair. As they were being intimate, Tang suddenly returned home and was furious. He punched and kicked Fuchang, giving him a beating. After neighbors intervened, Fuchang fled. However, not long after Fuchang left, several uninvited guests suddenly arrived at Tang's house and forcibly dragged Kun out. Yuan Fuchang was also waiting outside and together they dragged Tang Kun to a deserted area across the river from the Jiatai Silk Factory. There, Fuchang used an axe to strike Kun twice on the back of his neck and the left side of his head, causing blood to flow profusely. The assailants, seeing their goal achieved, fled. Kun, despite his injuries, pursued them. Near the Longchang Silk Factory, the assailant Yuan Fuchang was captured by people from the workshop and handed over to the police, who took him to the First Precinct of the Public Security Bureau for interrogation and detention. The other assailants escaped. Tang was rushed to the Brothers Hospital for treatment, but due to the fractured skull, his survival is doubtful.

Rice Store Accountant Flees with Large Sum of Money 105

The Yongsheng Rice Store in Sanli Bridge, Beiting, was jointly opened by Wu Yunxi, Wu Yaoting, and Feng Haoxi, and has been in business for nearly ten years. Feng Haoxi served as manager, and the business was thriving. The store's accountant, Zhu Zhongming, in his twenties, was usually cautious in his work. However, he was addicted to gambling and liked to frequent prostitutes, leading him to embezzle over 300 yuan from the store. Recently, he had a sudden idea and, at 9 AM yesterday, withdrew 5,000 yuan in cash from the Xingye Bank, with which the store regularly did business, and fled. After manager Feng Haoxi noticed, he sent people to various places, including Beijing, Shanghai, Wucheng, to search for him, but so far there has been no news of him.

Changzhou County Government Sends Official to Province to Organize Work Relief 106

The Wuyi County Government sent Shi Ziquan, chief of the third section, to the province the day before yesterday to meet with Shen Baixian, Director of the Construction Department. He stated that the disaster victims in the four rural areas of the county were suffering from hunger and cold, and it was urgently necessary to organize work relief to dredge the river, which could help some of the disaster victims. He requested that funds be allocated immediately for the organization. The Department stated that the funds for work relief to dredge the river were only 400,000 yuan and had to be distributed among 36 counties. With too few resources for too many monks, the documents requesting funds from various counties have not yet been approved. Director Shen promised that the funds could be distributed to various counties after Director Zhao returned to the province. However, for Wujin, the Department could allocate at least 40,000 yuan to be effective. After Section Chief Shi returned to Chang, he began to organize work relief to dredge the river starting yesterday (the 18th). It is planned to first selectively dredge the northern section of Baihe, Tongzi, and Sanshan Port, as well as the Zhi Canal. Technicians Jiang Tong and Yu Mengyin were sent to the above rivers to survey and design. Work is expected to begin in early next month.

Jiashan Captures Large Number of Bandits 108

In the Tianjing Port area, on the border between Xitang and Jinze, there were eight Jiangbei shacks. Township Chief Zhang Ziming, seeing their suspicious appearance, immediately reported to the Jinze Town Public Security Bureau. The police were dispatched to search them and immediately arrested 25 male and female bandits, including Zhou Jinnu, along with one copper handgun, two sharp knives, five cotton quilts, and three large bundles of clothing, including a blood-stained garment. The Public Security Bureau Chief considered the matter to be important and conducted a preliminary interrogation. Bank Run Occurs at Jiaxing Local Branch 109

The Jiaxing Local Bank branch is also in charge of the county treasury and issues banknotes, which are not small in number. Recently, after the He Di Three Qian Zhuang and one bank successively announced liquidation, outsiders suddenly made various rumors, causing a run on the bank's banknotes starting in the afternoon of the 18th, which was even more severe on the 19th. Fortunately, the bank was well-prepared, and those who presented banknotes for redemption were given cash. Therefore, the redemption was scarce in the afternoon. Merchants in the market also continued to accept the banknotes as usual. The county government also issued a notice on the 19th, ordering the bank to prepare sufficient cash to continue redemption and ordering tax collectors to continue accepting the banknotes.

Haimen Registers Victims of Baohua Ship Incident 110

The Ping An Company's Baohua Ship caused incidents on September 12th and 20th in Qi Dong Sanhe Port and Chongming Miao Port, respectively, drowning many passengers and losing countless goods. The families of the victims filed claims with the company, but to no avail. They then obtained approval from the Qi Dong County Government to detain the ship. The ship was later released on bail by the Shanghai Shipping Association, but the company delayed and ignored the compensation for damages. Yesterday, the Haimen Qi Beiyuan Public Support Association notified the families of the victims and the affected passengers to register with the association at Songshan Road, Shanghai, within one week to facilitate joint handling of the case.

Foreign Exchange Stabilization Committee Established Yesterday 111

Jointly Formed by Central, China, and Communications Banks

Initial Fund of 100 Million Yuan Already Raised

To avoid drastic fluctuations in the foreign exchange market after the increase in silver export tax, financial leaders requested the financial authorities to establish a Foreign Exchange Stabilization Committee, jointly formed by the Central, China, and Communications Banks. Each bank sent one representative as a member: Central Bank's Xi Demao, China Bank's Bei Songsun, and Communications Bank's Zhang Peishen. It was officially established yesterday, with an initial fund of 100 million yuan already raised. Details are as follows:

Continued Discussions in the Morning 112

At 12:15 PM yesterday, Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi continued discussions with financial leaders at the Central Bank on the Bund, third floor. Those present included Vice President Chen Jian'an of the Central Bank, Manager Xi Demao of the Business Bureau, Manager Bei Songsun of the China Bank, Coordinator Zhang Peishen of the Communications Bank, General Manager Song Ziliang of the China National Goods Bank, and General Manager Li Fusun of the Zhejiang Industrial Bank. The name "Foreign Exchange Stabilization Committee" was decided, with an initial fund of 100 million yuan, jointly formed by the Central, China, and Communications Banks. The members were Xi Demao of the Central Bank, Bei Songsun of the China Bank, and Zhang Peishen of the Communications Bank. The meeting ended at 1:30 PM.

Established in the Afternoon 113

The Foreign Exchange Stabilization Committee held its first committee meeting at 5:00 PM yesterday in the conference room on the third floor of the Central Bank on the Bund, announcing its establishment. The members present were Xi Demao of the Central Bank, Bei Songsun of the China Bank, and Zhang Peishen of the Communications Bank. The meeting ended at 5:45 PM. It is reported that the committee began work immediately after its establishment, without holding a ceremony. The Central Bank continued to post exchange rates as usual. In the past, although exchange rates were posted, they were not actual transaction rates (NOM). Now, importers and exporters who wish to trade will generally no longer be restricted.

Jiangsu Provincial Bonds Pledged for 10 Million Yuan 116

Interest at 8%, Term Temporarily Set at One Year

2 Million Yuan to Redeem Old Pledge Loans

According to Xin Sheng She, after the issuance of the 20 million yuan Jiangsu Water Conservancy Construction Bonds in 1934, Zhao Dihua, Director of the Jiangsu Finance Department, came to Shanghai to host a banquet for financial leaders to discuss pledges. An agreement has now been reached with the financial industry. Details are as follows:

Agreement on Pledge 117

After Zhao Dihua, Director of the Jiangsu Finance Department, hosted a banquet for financial leaders to discuss pledging the Water Conservancy Construction Bonds for loans, Director Zhao separately contacted various banks and qianzhuang to confirm the amount. The banks included the Central, China, Communications, Zhongnan, Continental, Salt Industry, Jincheng, Shanghai, and Jiangsu Farmers Banks. Total of 10 Million 118

Among them, 2 million yuan is to redeem the old account of the first phase of 4 million yuan of construction bonds previously issued by Jiangsu Province and pledged to banks for 2 million yuan. De Kang Gold Shop Collapses Amid Soaring Marker Gold Prices 120

Losses Estimated at Around 20,000 Yuan

Since the Ministry of Finance increased the silver export tax, the price of marker gold has soared daily. A large number of speculators in the financial market have suffered huge losses. Therefore, the De Kang Gold Shop at No. 69 Jiujiang Road suddenly collapsed yesterday. Fortunately, the shop acted as an agent for customers in the gold exchange, so the impact on other parties was small. Xin Ruikang, the owner of the shop, stated that the losses were estimated at around 20,000 yuan. The reason for the collapse was entirely due to the sudden surge in the price of marker gold on the 17th and 18th, causing the margin to be unpayable. The notice issued by the Gold Exchange is recorded as follows: (1) De Kang Gold Shop has not cleared its margin and should be temporarily suspended from business. This notice is issued. (2) De Kang Gold Shop has now been temporarily suspended from business. As of the close of the market on the 18th, there were still seven marker gold short positions. The Exchange has designated Fu Tai Xiang Gold Shop to settle them today in accordance with the rules of business. This notice is issued.

International Trade Bureau Informs Chamber of Commerce of Tax Reduction on Silk Exports to England 121

The International Trade Bureau sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday, stating: "According to Instruction No. 28251 from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has consulted that the Consulate General in Liverpool has reported that the French government suddenly reduced the number of English coal imports at the beginning of February of this year, and England immediately increased tariffs on French goods. The French government, motivated by domestic tension, considered abolishing the commercial treaties signed between England and France in 1826 and 1822. A new treaty has now been negotiated and will take effect on July 1st. Until April 1st of next year, during this period, the number of English coal shipments to France will be fully restored, and the 20% increase in tariffs on French goods to England will also be cancelled. At the same time, England will reduce tariffs on silk, rayon, vegetables, and other items. The tariff on silk has now been reduced, and China can enjoy the same treatment under the most-favored-nation clause. The three copies of the English-French commercial treaty, the abolition of the old treaty, and the three copies of the exchange of letters are attached for reference. Please forward them to the Ministry of Finance and Commerce. The relevant items are attached and sent to your Ministry to be forwarded to the chambers of commerce in various places to pay attention to the reduction of tax rates enjoyed by Chinese silk imported into England and French silk. This order, etc., is issued. Accordingly, the tax rate schedule in the commercial treaty is translated into Chinese and attached to this letter for reference. Please forward it so that everyone can pay attention." The Silk Tariff section of the first part of the tax rate schedule is excerpted below: (1) Silk cocoons and waste silk, not bleached, six pence per hundredweight if wholly or partly bleached (excluding short-fiber waste silk); short-fiber waste silk, six pence. (2) Raw silk, not bleached, one shilling six pence; wholly or partly bleached, two shillings two pence. (3) Silk yarn, not bleached, two shillings two pence; wholly or partly bleached (excluding spun silk), two shillings nine pence; spun silk, nine pence.

City Chamber of Commerce Submits to the Executive Yuan Requesting Postponement of New Stamp Tax Law 122

The law violates the principles determined by the Central Political Council.

Please revise it carefully to reduce the burden on merchants.

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce submitted a report to the Executive Yuan yesterday, stating: Regarding the draft stamp tax law prepared by the Legislative Yuan, it has been reported that it was passed by the 73rd Yuan meeting on October 12th. Article 16 stipulates the documents subject to stamp tax and the tax rates. Among them, (1) delivery notes, (2) receipts for money and goods, and (3) bills are all subject to a stamp tax of one cent for each amount of three yuan or more but less than ten yuan, and an additional stamp tax of one cent for each additional ten yuan, but with a maximum limit of one yuan. According to the current stamp tax regulations, Article 2 stipulates that delivery notes are subject to a stamp tax of one cent regardless of the amount, and money receipts are subject to one cent for less than ten yuan and two cents for ten yuan or more. Comparing the new tax law with the current regulations, the maximum tax amount for delivery notes has increased by 100 times, and the tax amount for receipts has increased by 50 times. The bill item is not included in the current regulations. It is true that merchants have already clearly stated the payable invoices in the invoices when selling goods. Except for hotels and restaurants, there are no independent bills. Now, a new item is also established, and stamp tax is added according to the amount up to one yuan. All of these are where the new tax law is heavier than the current regulations, but it is inappropriate in terms of reason, commercial affairs, and situation. The Central Political Council is the highest political authority and has the power to create and formulate. Therefore, whenever a law is drafted, the Central Political Council first formulates legislative principles and hands them over to the Legislative Yuan to draft detailed articles. It is clear that the Legislative Yuan should not have contrary provisions to the legislative principles formulated by the Central Political Council. According to Article 5 of the stamp tax law principles formulated by the Central Political Council last year, those with more significant evidence of validity or rights, or those used for a long time, should be taxed heavily, while those with less significant evidence of validity or rights, or those used for a short time, should be taxed lightly. Article 6 states that documents for frequent behaviors should mostly adopt a simple and easy fixed-amount tax, and documents for rare behaviors should mostly adopt an easy-to-calculate progressive tax. Delivery notes, bills, and receipts are the most common documents for merchants and are daily behaviors, which are completely different from the subletting documents, stock certificates, joint venture business documents, and corporate bond tickets listed in the appendix to the law, which are documents for rare behaviors. Now, progressive tax is also levied on documents for common behaviors, the same as subletting documents, etc., which violates the principles formulated by the Central Political Council. Also, if the goods and payments for invoices, receipts, bills, etc. are settled immediately, the time of validity of the documents is extremely short. In addition, those who settle accounts at the end of the month, whether it is a large or small month, have a validity of only half a month or a month. Those who settle accounts at the end of the year have a validity of only three festivals, which is completely different from the significance and long validity of the rights of subletting documents, stock certificates, and joint venture business documents. Now, the tax amount is increased by 50 times or 100 times compared with the current regulations, which is disproportionate and violates the principles formulated by the Central Political Council. In addition to the fact that the affiliated association had previously telegraphed the Central Political Council on the 12th of this month to request correction, Article 24 of the association states that the date of implementation of this law shall be determined by order. Before the Central Political Council corrects this tax law based on the stamp tax law principles formulated last year, we would like to request your Yuan to submit it to the National Government for temporary non-promulgation and implementation by order, so that it can be revised carefully. This matter is related to maintaining the principles of national legislation and reducing the undue burden on merchants, and is of utmost urgency. We respectfully submit it to the Executive Yuan.

Unemployed Overseas Chinese from the Netherlands Transported by Hai Yuan Ship 125

Approved to arrive in Shanghai on November 2nd

The first Hai Yuan ship newly built by the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company set sail from England on September 14th. According to the speed of the ship, it could reach Shanghai in 35 days. Now, when departing from England, the Chinese Embassy in England received instructions from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. In recent years, overseas Chinese in the Netherlands have suffered from the global commercial depression. Those who stay in various places in the Netherlands have not only lost their ability to do business, but the Dutch authorities have also restricted the entry of overseas Chinese due to the increasing number of unemployed in the country. Those who have already been engaged in business and work in the country have been subjected to even stricter crackdowns, resulting in all the overseas Chinese stranded in the Netherlands having their livelihoods cut off and being unable to return to their country. They have asked the envoys and consuls stationed in the country to telegraph the central government to find ways to provide relief. The central government immediately ordered the Ministry of Communications to inform Wu Daming, the commissioner of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company stationed in England for supervising the construction of new ships, and to notify the embassy stationed in England to order him to go to the Netherlands to carry this large group of overseas Chinese back to China when the first new Hai Yuan ship built by the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company in England returns to China. However, when Hai Yuan left England, it did not report this intention to the bureau in a telegram. After departing from London, it went to the Netherlands to load this large group of expelled unemployed overseas Chinese and return to their country. The bureau was deeply worried about the delay in the arrival of the Hai Yuan ship because it did not know about this matter. Fang Ziwei of the Radio Station once telegraphed all the Hai Yuan ships of the bureau near Hong Kong to call out. Because the short wave could not reach Shanghai directly. There was no response the first time. It was not until the second time that it was called. The Hai Yuan ship had already gone from England to the Netherlands. After carrying a large number of overseas Chinese, it sailed along the Indian Ocean. Yesterday, the Hai Yuan ship had telegraphed Shanghai, saying, "This ship has now reached 89 degrees 15 minutes east longitude and 5 degrees 50 minutes north latitude. If there are no major storms along the way, it is expected to arrive in Shanghai on November 2nd with overseas Chinese living in the Netherlands." After receiving the telegram, the bureau's shipping department had prepared to send a telegram to Hong Kong when the ship arrives, asking for the exact date of import to Shanghai, so that the bureau could send a pilot to Tongsha to lead the new ship to Jinliyuan Wharf to dock. Because the Hai Yuan has a definite date of arrival in Shanghai, Liu Hongsheng telegraphed the Ministry of Communications yesterday to ask what name to use for the new ship to entertain people from all walks of life to visit. Soon, he received a reply from the Ministry, saying that the Hai Yuan's arrival in Shanghai for entertainment should be approved in the name of the Ministry of Communications. Minister Zhu will also come to Shanghai to preside over the event. The Ministry of Communications also notified the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission of the date of arrival of the Hai Yuan ship that rescued the Dutch overseas Chinese and asked it to send personnel to Jinliyuan Wharf at that time to take care of everything.

After the Increased Export Tax on Silver, Gu Xinyi Discusses the Market Situation of Miscellaneous Grains 127

Wheat flour prices rise, the exchange pursues margin payments

Domestic agricultural products sell well, and farmers benefit

According to the Central News Agency, since the Ministry of Finance announced the increase in export tax on silver, the market situation of various goods transactions in this city has shown a sharp increase. The Central News Agency reporter specially visited Gu Xinyi, chairman of the Miscellaneous Grains Association of this city, to inquire about the market situation of miscellaneous grains. According to the interview as follows:

Wheat Flour Prices Rise According to Gu, the market prices of miscellaneous grains and flour in this city have shown a decline since autumn, and foreign goods have taken advantage of the opportunity to dump them, and there is even a possibility of a complete collapse. However, since the Ministry of Finance announced the increase in export tax on silver due to the recent sharp increase in the number of silver exports from China, the number of silver exports itself can be reduced. Foreign goods are affected by this, and market prices increase. For example, for wheat, there were originally sales from countries such as Canada to China. Assuming the original price was two yuan, but after the export tax on silver is levied, the price must also be increased at the same time. Therefore, the domestic market price has also increased.

Pursuing Margin Payments In recent days, the price of various commodities in the market has risen sharply. Therefore, the exchanges also need to increase the payment of margin. It has now been decided that the margin payable for every 1,000 bags of wheat will be increased to 500 yuan, and the margin payable for every 500 dan of flour will be increased to 400 yuan. Now, the short position margin is being pursued, and bidding has been temporarily suspended. After all the short position margin has been paid, bidding will be reopened.

Prices Looking High Gu also said that, according to the current situation, the prices of various commodities still have a tendency to continue to rise. The government also plans to levy a balancing tax after the export tax. Now, a balancing committee is about to be established in this city. After converting the London silver market price and the local market price, the difference will be used to levy the balancing tax, so that the silver export price in this city is equal to the London market price. Therefore, after the balancing tax on silver is increased, the prices of various commodities will continue to rise.

Farmers Benefit Gu concluded that this time, the government resolutely levied export tax and balancing tax on silver, so that the prices of various commodities can increase. Merchants deeply sympathize with the government's move. In rural areas, the prices of various agricultural products have also increased, so foreign goods can be resisted from entering, and domestic agricultural products can be sold well. Therefore, farmers can also benefit a lot in their lives. Now that it has just been implemented, there will inevitably be slight fluctuations in the market, but it will soon be stable.

The First Batch of Shaanxi Cotton Will Be Shipped to Shanghai 128

Quality is higher than before

According to news from the Cotton Industry Control Committee of the National Economic Commission yesterday, the cotton production in Shaanxi Province has greatly improved after the province has made great efforts to promote it. New cotton has now entered the harvest season. The Cotton Production, Transportation, and Sales Cooperative, guided by the Shaanxi Cotton Production Improvement Institute, specially sent a letter to the Cotton Control Committee requesting that five experienced cotton graders be sent to the province to carry out cotton grading work. There are currently sixteen cotton production, transportation, and sales cooperatives in Shaanxi, distributed in Sanyuan, Jingyang, Weinan, Huazhou, and other counties, which are famous for cotton production, with a total of about 200,000 mu of cotton fields, with an estimated cotton production of about 50,000 dan. The cotton graders sent by the Cotton Control Committee will be assigned to work in the above-mentioned areas. Before the cotton is packed, the grades will be determined and identified, and the grade level and length will be noted on the package, and then it will be directly transported and sold for the convenience of various yarn factories to purchase. According to a recent letter from the graders to the cooperative, the cotton grade level and length are about between medium and high grade, and the length is about from 13/16 to 15/16 inches. Therefore, the quality is higher than that produced in previous years. It is heard that the first batch of graded cotton will be shipped to Shanghai soon, and it is predictable that it will be welcomed by various yarn factories. In addition, the Central Cotton Adulteration and Mixing Prohibition Institute, which is affiliated to the committee, received a communication from the Shaan County branch of the Henan Adulteration and Mixing Prohibition Institute yesterday, saying that the Shaan County branch of the Henan Cotton Adulteration and Mixing Prohibition Institute recently discovered a batch of cotton adulterated with water and impurities and a water gun in a packaging factory. They were sent to the Commissioner's Office for investigation and handling according to law. It is heard that the case was sentenced to three months in prison and fined 800 yuan as a warning.

Jiangsu Stamp Tax Sub-bureaus Jointly Petition to Return the Remaining Stamps 131

Since the Ministry of Finance announced the order to abolish and replace the stamp tax tickets, the local sub-bureaus have been unable to sell the stamps they have been claiming on a monthly basis, because there are already too many stamps in the business community, and there is no way out at all. However, the original order of the Ministry of Finance states that "all the stamp tax tickets that have been claimed but not sold by the bureau and its subordinates should be compiled into a clear list and submitted to the Ministry." It is generally believed that the remaining stamps can be returned after the end, and the capital can be recovered. However, the provincial bureau submitted a report to the Ministry, and then added restrictions, only allowing those who claimed in October to return them. In fact, in these consecutive off-seasons, very few sub-bureaus in various places have claimed as late as August and September, let alone October. The above-mentioned restrictive measures are tantamount to declaring that the sub-bureaus are not allowed to return the remaining stamps. Therefore, the sub-bureaus, with the same environment and accumulating remaining stamps, were all panicked and exchanged letters and telegrams to discuss relief measures. Recently, a joint office of sub-bureaus across the province was organized at No. 61, Lane 576, Yuyuan Road, West Shanghai. Recently, the heads of the sub-bureaus gathered in Shanghai for a meeting. Everyone believed that the sub-bureaus in this province were all appointment-based and did not contain the nature of a contractor who recognized the amount and contracted sales, and did not bear any liability for compensation at all. Moreover, the cancellation was at the beginning of the peak season, which prevented the sub-bureaus from adjusting the surplus to make up for the expenses. Forcing them to compensate for the sales of the remaining stamps was too harsh. On the spot, Xi Yin Shi Ruiting, Nantong Ge Songting, Wu County Xie Zuxi, and Nan Fengchuan Ma Haishan were elected as representatives of the entire group to petition the provincial bureau, requesting to return the remaining stamps, reissue the expenses, and request severance pay as an example. At the same time, it was resolved that the transfer would not be made until the goal was achieved, and further petitions would be made.

Banks Have Paid Up Savings Guarantee Securities 132

In order to implement the bank savings law, the Ministry of Finance ordered all banks to organize a savings deposit guarantee reserve management committee, and ordered all banks to deposit one-quarter of the savings in various securities with the Central Bank for safekeeping, in order to protect the interests of depositors. It is now known that all banks have paid up this guarantee certificate, with a total amount of approximately 80 million yuan. However, some of the securities, etc., that have been paid in are still under review by the management committee. It is also known that the committee will notify each bank to make up for the securities at any time when the market price of the securities fluctuates, and vice versa, but the amount of the change is at least five yuan, so as to avoid the trouble of small refunds. Also, if the total amount of savings in each bank changes, it will be increased or decreased every six months according to the accounts of each bank.

Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce Industrial and Commercial Laws and Regulations Research Committee 133

Resolved to Draft Measures to Compel the Industry to Join the Guild

The Industrial and Commercial Laws and Regulations Research Committee of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce held its third plenary committee meeting on the 18th. The committee members present were Li Wenjie, Fang Jiaobo, Wang Xiaowen, Wang Xiaotong, Xi Yushu, Sun Xiaolou, Xu Yongzuo, Cao Zhigong, Zhang Zhengxue (substituting for Xu Yongzuo), Pan Xulun, Xie Chunpu (substituting for Li Wenjie), and other ten people. The meeting was chaired by the standing committee members Fang Jiaobo and Li Wenjie to discuss the following matters: (1) The Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a letter requesting to formulate sanctions against industrial and commercial companies and firms that do not join the same trade association, in order to petition the central government to include them in the Chamber of Commerce Law and the Trade Association Law. First, Li Wenjie reported on the process of handling the case by the committee and the content obtained from reviewing the files over the years. It was resolved that, after investigating the Industrial and Commercial Trade Association Law, it originally took the principle that members could join the association at will. The Legislative Yuan changed the word "may" in Article 7 of the law to "shall." The sanctions against non-members were not included in the article, so that the meaning of the law and the text of the law could not be matched. The spirit of the compulsory membership system could not be fully utilized. In addition, such as the implementation rules of the Industrial and Commercial Trade Association Law, the articles of association of various trade associations, and the regulations of various industries, many of the provisions are not compatible with the current meaning of the law, and it is necessary to plan for them as a whole. Therefore, (A) the committee should send a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to collect the regulations of each industry and the articles of association of each trade association and send them to the committee. (B) Sun Xiaolou, Xi Yushu, Cao Zhigong, and Li Wenjie were appointed to formulate a number of effective measures to compel the industry to join the association based on the information. (C) All committee members will be notified again to express their opinions within a certain period. (D) Finally, the standing committee members will synthesize the opinions of all parties and formulate a specific plan to respond to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce. (2) The Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a letter from Executive Committee Member Xiao Die to Standing Committee Member Zheqing Chen, which should be studied together. It was resolved that Chen's opinion did not involve the scope of legal research, so the results of the factual research should be added to the opinion and responded to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce. (A) It should be handled by the organization section of the Commercial Affairs Department. (B) It is in line with the provisions of Article 10 of the Implementation Rules of the Industrial and Commercial Trade Association Law, and the organization section of the Commercial Affairs Department should also pay attention to it. (C) It is absolutely impossible to send the industry regulations to the Legislative Yuan for review and approval. (D) Omitted. (E) This is the responsibility of the product display center. (3) Committee Member Li Wenjie proposed that the Shanghai Lawyers Association petitioned the government to abolish the Shanghai Real Estate Mortgage Registration Rules. After investigating that the Land Bureau is the land administration agency of this city, and the land registry and measurement map data of this city are all in the hands of the bureau, there are places where the mortgage registration of real estate must be demanded from the Land Bureau in particular. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce should petition the Ministry of Justice to pay attention to the characteristics of the land practice certificate in this city. Except for the part of the real estate mortgage registration rules that conflict with the provisions of the Civil Law, the court and the Land Bureau should still be responsible for cooperating in handling real estate rights registration matters before the Land Law is implemented. (Resolved) Passed, and responded to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce.

Photographic Record of the Drought Disaster in Huzhou 134

Disaster area covers six counties

Nearly one million disaster victims

Huzhou has always been known as a rich area, but due to years of disasters, the silk industry has plummeted, and the livelihood of farmers has been on the verge of collapse. This year, it has also encountered a strange drought, and the fields in the four villages have become barren. Even if there is a lucky harvest, the wages for bailing water are too high, and it is not worth the loss. Now, wailing is everywhere, and the hungry are waiting to be fed. The local public funds of each county have long been embezzled. Although there is a desire for relief, there is a lack of magic. They can only telegraph the disaster situation to the outside world and ask for relief. In recent days, the Huzhou Relief Committee in this city has received telegrams from various groups in the six counties of Huzhou requesting relief, which are like snowflakes flying in. The committee is concerned about its hometown and has a sense of justice. On the one hand, it distributes donation booklets and strives to raise donations. On the other hand, it appeals to the Zhejiang authorities for relief. The day before yesterday, Tian Xin, the deputy director of the committee, was selected to attend the Zhejiang Relief Meeting in Hangzhou and returned two days ago. According to him, the provincial government has agreed with the banking group to borrow 600,000 yuan for relief funds for distribution. However, there are more than 60 counties in Zhejiang Province, and the disaster situation is generally very serious. The small amount of funds seems difficult to help. Therefore, after Shen reported on the situation of attending the meeting, he is now trying to raise more donations in order to prevent the people of his hometown from becoming displaced. Now, the disaster situation in the six counties of Huzhou has been investigated and recorded as follows: (Wuxing) The total area of cultivated land in the county is 2,089,000 mu, and the disaster area is 627,000 mu, accounting for 30% of the total.

(Disaster situation (Severe drought for months, branches and ports have become streams, uncultivated fields have been turned into stones, and most of the cultivated rice has turned yellow and withered. Even if there is a slight harvest, it is not worth the loss due to the excessive wages for bailing water. There are more than 300,000 disaster victims, who are filling their stomachs with water chestnut seedlings and taro stems. Some have even committed suicide in anger because they have nothing to eat, or have forcibly grabbed food and touched the criminal law. There have been many cases. (Changxing) The total area of cultivated land in the county is 1,343,000 mu, and the disaster area is 873,000 mu, accounting for 65% of the total. (Disaster situation) The county borders the mountains and the lake. Mountain fields cannot be bailed for relief and have become barren. At first, the lake fields tried hard to pump water, not hesitating to pawn and borrow to pay for wages. Then, the river and port were dry, and pumping for relief was impossible. Taihu Building Port is either blocked and impassable, or the mouth is deep and wide and cannot be stored. Although there is a vast ocean, it cannot be used, and the fields and rice are watched to wither. Moreover, because there was water to pump at the beginning, pawning and borrowing was done in order to save it. The pain of the disaster area near the lake is even greater. There are now more than 200,000 disaster victims, who are scrambling for grass roots and bark to fill their stomachs, and selling their daughters in the market to exchange for liters of rice. (Deqing) The total area of cultivated land in the county is 549,000 mu, and the disaster area is 357,000 mu, accounting for 65% of the total. (Disaster situation) There is no way to sow uncultivated fields, and the rice that has been planted has withered. Although efforts have been made to pump water for relief, it is impossible to limit the height and position of the land, and the water flows downwards. Those near the water can barely survive, while those in high places cannot draw water. Most of the thousands of acres of good land have been turned into stones, and most of the farmland in the four villages is barren. Although it rained at the beginning of autumn, it was too late. Although the withered rice has recovered, it is all showy but not fruitful. The miscellaneous grains that have been replanted are seedlings but not showy. There are more than 100,000 disaster victims, and their food is not sustainable, and their lives are in danger. (Anji) The total area of cultivated land in the county is 512,000 mu, and the disaster area is 358,000 mu, accounting for 70% of the total. (Disaster situation) The whole county is located in the mountains, and there are many mountain fields. This year's severe drought has caused all the rice, millet, and potatoes to wither and die. Although there were effective drought prevention measures beforehand, 90% of the mountain and ridge fields could not be irrigated for relief, resulting in no harvest. There are 100,000 disaster victims, who are picking ferns to fill their stomachs and plucking quinoa to fill their intestines. (Wukang) The total area of cultivated land in the county is 234,000 mu, and the disaster area is 234,000 mu, accounting for 100% of the total. (Disaster situation) The planted rice seedlings have withered, and the uncultivated farmland is cracked. Other miscellaneous grains, such as sweet potatoes, taro, and corn, have all withered and died. Even the large and small Mao bamboo in the mountains have died mostly due to prolonged dryness, which will affect production in the coming year. Moreover, several dikes and ponds in various places have collapsed due to excessive dryness. 60,000 disaster victims are suffering from hunger and cold, and their lives are in danger. (Xiaofeng) The total area of cultivated land in the county is 309,000 mu, and the disaster area is 222,000 mu, accounting for 72% of the total. (Disaster situation) Severe drought for months, mountain valleys have become streams, and the fields in small valleys and hills have become barren. There are 100,000 wailing victims waiting to be fed, and incidents of robbing food and committing suicide are heard every day.

### One Dead Sailor and One Passenger on the Xinfeng Ship Traveling Between Tianjin and Shanghai 136

The China Merchants Bureau's regular Beiyang ship, the Xinfeng, which departed from Tianjin, experienced an incident on the 15th of this month at 3:00 AM when the ship left the Dagu estuary. At 8:30 AM, it had reached the sea, and the ship was traveling very fast. A third-class passenger on the ship suddenly went from the third-class cabin to the first-class deck. At this time, the sea wind was quite strong, and the passenger, taking advantage of the lack of preparation, suddenly jumped into the sea to commit suicide. Inspector Li Mengsheng caught a glimpse of this and immediately tried to rescue him, but it was too late. He immediately reported to the administrative office, Wang Jiwu, and notified the ship owner to stop the ship immediately. Lifeboats were quickly lowered to rescue the passenger, and after he surfaced twice, he was rescued. However, by the time he was brought back on board, he had already died of suffocation due to being in the water for too long. On-site inspection revealed the passenger's name to be Jiang Defa, 40 years old. The reason for the suicide is unknown. The deceased was found to have eight yuan and nine jiao in silver coins and three hundred wen in cash. He also had a basket containing a washbasin, towel, and toothbrush cup. The deceased was wearing a Chinese-style cotton robe and a black cloth jacket. The Xinfeng ship carried the body to Yantai, where it docked at the Shengde pier. The body was transferred ashore and reported to the court for inspection. It will be temporarily stored in a coffin at Guangshiyuan, and if no one claims it within two months, it will be buried at the bureau's expense. The bureau received the report yesterday and ordered its branches to investigate the deceased's family and claim the body and belongings.

Another bizarre incident occurred on the Xinfeng ship. According to the sailor foreman, Wang Xiaoda, a sailor named Liu Ahua suddenly went missing from the sailor's section of the Xinfeng ship during its trip from Shanghai to Tianjin and back. A thorough search was conducted, but he could not be found. All the sailors said that Liu Ahua was still on board when the ship departed and that he was ill. It is possible that the sailor was working on deck at night when the ship was sailing in the Beiyang sea and was swept into the sea by the wind and waves. A request for compensation has been submitted to the head office.
