Orphanage Exhibition Judging Completed 138

Location: Zhabei Civilian Education Center

After the conclusion of the National Child Welfare Conference, the China Child Welfare Association sent all the child welfare items contributed by various regions to the Liuying Road branch of the Zhabei Civilian Education Center. The association then sent letters to the nine judging committee members recommended by the conference, requesting them to conduct the judging at the Zhabei Civilian Education Center at 3:00 PM yesterday. Wang Xiaolai, Zhao Jinqing, Zhu Shaoyang, Chen Liting, Ding Shujing, Zhu Lide, Chen Tiesheng, and other committee members, as well as secretaries Zhou Chucai, Jiang Zhuoying, He Qi, and others, more than ten people in total, were present. Shujing was elected as the chairman, and judging standards were agreed upon: (1) Focus on practical handicrafts; (2) handicrafts were divided into three categories: superior, special, and excellent, and certificates were issued by the conference; (3) charts, statistical tables, and photographs were given certificates of appreciation by the conference. The committee members then proceeded to judge all the exhibits displayed in the hall of the center one by one. As a result, the items that won superior awards included the woolen yarn from the Hankou Orphanage, the gauze from the Zhenjiang Orphanage, the cloth from the Henan Relief Institute and Disaster Children's Education Center, the lacquerware from the Fujian Hui'er Institute, and the bronzeware from the Zhabei Civilian Education Center. The items that won special awards included the hot-stamped screens from the Hubei Relief Institute, the felt rugs from the Ningbo Orphanage, the leather crafts and pottery pencils from the Xiangshan Child Welfare Institute, and the medicated cotton from the Xi'an Orphanage Education Center, etc. The remaining items were all listed as excellent. It is reported that a total of 42 institutions participated. The judging committee members agreed that (1) the China Child Welfare Association would be responsible for the custody of all exhibits that institutions wished to keep as permanent memorials; (2) the China Child Welfare Association would be responsible for collecting the proceeds from the sale of exhibits that institutions wished to sell and returning the money to the original institutions. The meeting adjourned at 5:00 PM with tea and refreshments.

Writer Ms. Luo Chen Arrives in Shanghai 142

Ms. Luo Chen, originally from Poland, is a highly accomplished writer and the wife of Mr. Hua Nan Gui, a pioneer in China's transportation industry. After coming to China, she wrote the book "Love and Obligation," which has been published in Chinese, English, and French. The Chinese and English versions were published by the Shanghai Commercial Press. In the form of a novel, it vividly depicts the conflict and distress between the old and new mentalities of young men and women in China's transitional era, as well as the drawbacks of uncritically adopting Western culture. It is truly a motto for Chinese youth. It was adapted into a film by a company in this country, and viewers were all moved. Her French title is Symphonie des Ombres Chinoises, published in Paris and sold by the Commercial Press. After reading this book, French intellectuals have changed their long-standing contempt for our country. Recently, she has written two new books, which will be published by the Commercial Press this year. One is a novel called "Double Practice," which describes the results of Chinese students sent abroad to study and the errors of this policy. It is quite thought-provoking to read. The other is a collection of essays called "Heart Writings," which are mostly aimed at the current state of Chinese society and offer many instructions for the behavior of young women in particular. Ms. Luo has come to Shanghai for a visit to discuss issues related to her writings.

Further Hearing in Chen Baoming Kidnapping Case Involving Female Bandit Hu Yaoshi 144

Verdict Expected on the 25th After Yesterday's Conclusion of the Interrogation

Chen Fengxiang, the late manager of the Pudong Nanmatou map company, was quite wealthy, which led to his being targeted by bandits. On the afternoon of July 10th of this year, at 10:00 PM, they took the opportunity to abduct Chen Fengxiang's sixteen-year-old son, Chen Baoming, in Xuja and hid him in the house of Hu Yaoshi in Zhoupu. Chen Baoming escaped back home when the bandit guarding him fell asleep. After the case was discovered, only Hu Yaoshi was arrested and brought to the local court for interrogation and prosecution by the criminal division. After the trial was held, it was not concluded. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Sun Jikang reopened the hearing. The victim, Chen Baoming, was not present, but Shen Dezhang was present as his representative. He testified that he was 66 years old, from Shanghai, and lived at Wujiaxing, Nanmatou, Pudong. (Judge) What is your relationship to Chen Baoming? (Answer) I am his relative. (Judge) Do you know about this matter? (Answer) I do. (Judge) When was Chen Baoming kidnapped? (Answer) On the night of July 10th. He was kidnapped on the road from the new house to the old house. (Judge) Who opened the door for Chen Baoming at Hu's house? (Answer) I don't know. (Judge) Do you know if Hu Yaoshi knew about the kidnapping at the time? (Answer) I don't know. (Judge) Who gave Chen Baoming food to eat? (Answer) Hu Yaoshi. (Judge) Who was guarding him? (Answer) Li Apei. (Judge) Did anyone see Chen Baoming escape? (Answer) Two children saw him. (Judge) Was A Hegen (Hu Yaoshi's husband) present at the scene of the kidnapping? (Answer) I don't know. (Judge) Why was the letter sent by the kidnappers not handed over to the authorities? (Answer) The letter is stored in the Public Security Bureau. (Judge) Is it true that Chen Baoming has gone to Nanjing? (Answer) No, not Nanjing. After escaping from the bandits, Wang Yiting introduced him to a school in Japan. Then Hu Yaoshi was asked, How did your husband know Li Apei? (Answer) They knew each other from when he sold eggs. (Judge) When did Chen Baoming, Li Apei, etc., come to your house? (Answer) I forgot. (Judge) Did your husband go with them? (Answer) I was wronged. (Judge) Where was your husband that day? (Answer) He was in the fields drawing water because of the drought. You can investigate that. I thought it was a normal thing. Who knew this kidnapping would happen? (Judge) How did Chen Baoming escape? (Answer) I went to the fields to help my husband draw water. I don't know. (Judge) Don't you worry about strangers in your house stealing things? (Answer) My house is very poor. There are no valuable things. (Judge) Did Li Apei come to your house to discuss it beforehand? (Answer) No, that's not true. I was really wronged. At this point, Prosecutor Tang Ruxiu made a statement, and then the defense began. Lawyer Tang Hao stood up and defended Hu Yaoshi for a long time, requesting that she be declared innocent. The judge considered the matter concluded and scheduled the verdict for the 25th of this month. Hu Yaoshi was returned to custody.

Several People Arrested for Smuggling Drugs 145

Hongkou Police Detective Chen Weikun and Detective Fang Fucheng were patrolling near Zha Pu Road at 9:15 PM the night before last when they saw two Cantonese men, Li Kangshan and Huang Bang, each carrying a paper bag. The bags were quite heavy, and their behavior was suspicious. They were stopped and taken to the police station. After reporting to the head of the police, the bags were opened and found to contain heroin. One bag weighed nine pounds, and the other weighed four and a half pounds. After questioning, it was learned that the drugs were given to them by a fellow villager named Zhao Gen, who lived at No. 6, Lane 360, Wuchang Road, to be transported to Guangdong and Hong Kong for sale. The detectives secretly went to the address and arrested a Cantonese woman, Huang Kuan. When asked where the drugs were hidden, she said that they were all in a wardrobe upstairs. They took the key, went upstairs, and opened the wardrobe, where they found three large bags of the same drugs, each weighing nine pounds, one small bag weighing four and a half pounds, a large can of red pills, counting several thousand, a seal, a ledger, twenty-four yuan in silver dollars, one yuan in cash, and more than ten yuan in coins. After a while, the Cantonese man Zhao Gen and Li Neng, who rented the house, arrived one after another and were arrested. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special Court. The lawyer of the Municipal Council, Li Zhishan, stated the facts and said that the defendants Li Kangshan and Huang Bang were sailors on a ship, and the mastermind, Wang Bing, was on the run. He requested that the case be postponed for further investigation. All the evidence was presented, and Judge Wu Zehan questioned the defendants and ordered them to be remanded in custody for further review at a later date.

Yue Lai Southern Goods Store Bombed 149

Five People Injured by Yesterday Afternoon's Bombing

Liang Tongfang Would Rather Die

The Yuelai Southern Goods Store at No. 356 Guangdong Road in the Public Concession of this city has been in business for a long time and has always been prosperous. It can be called one of the leading southern goods merchants in this city. The owner, Gong Fanglai, has been bombed once before, and the news has spread throughout the country. Gong actually took his anger out on the newspaper vendors who sell newspapers and arrested them in court, accusing them of interfering with his business. However, after the court trial, they were declared not guilty. Yesterday afternoon, someone went to bomb the store again, injuring five people on the spot. The details are described below:

A Loud Bang Occurred at 12:10 PM Yesterday Afternoon

Around 12:10 PM yesterday afternoon, when most of the store's staff were having lunch in the back of the store, a young man suddenly came to the entrance, wearing a Zhongshan suit and carrying a paper bag under his left arm. After standing in front of the counter, he put a paper bag wrapped in newspaper on the counter. The store's staff thought it was a customer and was about to come forward to greet him when the paper bag suddenly exploded with a loud bang, sending iron shrapnel flying in all directions. The young man, three store staff members, and one customer were injured at the same time. Several pieces of glass next to the counter were also shattered.

The Bombing Youth After the bomb exploded, the young man turned and ran out. However, because his movements were slow, his left and right hands were severely injured. He managed to run to the entrance of the Kongming Electrical Appliance Store across the street before finally collapsing due to his injuries. At the same time, nearby neighbors heard the sound and came to investigate. After learning the details, they all stopped to watch. Nearby policemen also arrived after hearing the alarm and immediately arrested the bombing youth. They reported the incident to the police station, which sent a car to take the three injured staff members, one customer, and the bombing youth to Renji Hospital for treatment.

Patriot Crippled It was learned that the bombing youth was Liang Tongfang, who had previously served in the Northeast Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army. After being demobilized and coming to Shanghai, he pulled a rickshaw for a living. Frustrated, he attempted suicide by taking poison at the Lao Dongfang Hotel on Hankou Road but was rescued. After being introduced, he studied at the Dongya Sports School in Xieqiao, Nanshi. Five fingers on his right hand had been blown off, and his left ring finger and little finger were also affected. The hospital considered his injuries to be critical and amputated his right hand. The other parts were bandaged. Due to the seriousness of the case, the police transferred him to the Municipal Council Hospital yesterday afternoon for surveillance. However, Liang will be crippled from now on.

List of the Injured The other injured persons are (1) Pan Hongchu, from Nanhui, injured his right hand and face; (2) Fu Yongsheng, from Nanhui, injured his left hand and left chest; (3) Ding Yanzhi, from Nanxiang, injured his head and face. All three were staff members of Yuelai Southern Goods Store. There was also one person named Pan Asan, who was a cook at the Tong Shen Customs Brokerage Company in Jinyu Dong Lane, Zhengjia Muqiao. He was going to buy dried shrimp for cooking noodles when he was injured. Fortunately, he was injured on his left hand, and the injuries were very minor. After Renji Hospital bandaged the wounds for each of them, they were discharged from the hospital. After the incident, the police went to investigate and sent two armed Chinese policemen to protect the entrance of the store. As for Liang's actions, he told people in the hospital that he would rather die.

Throat and Pediatrician Dr. Zhu Ziyun Sued 150

Cai Zirong Accuses Him of Negligence Causing Death

Plaintiff Fails to Appear at the Trial

Zhu Ziyun, a well-known throat and pediatric specialist in traditional Chinese medicine, is from Jiangwan. He is 45 years old and has been practicing medicine for 25 years. His clinic is located at No. 447 Zhoujiazu Road, Hongkou, and his business is booming. He sees more than 200 patients a day. He has been targeted by bandits, and both kidnapping and robbery have occurred. Unexpectedly, he was recently sued by Cai Zirong, who lives at No. 26 Yisong Lane, Tokyo Road, in the Criminal Court of the First Special District Court, accusing Zhu of committing the crime of negligence causing death under Article 291, Section 2 of the Criminal Law, requesting that he be punished according to the law. The facts are as follows: Cai Zirong had a son, Shunbao, who was less than 30 months old. In July of this year, he suddenly developed measles. On the 16th of this month, he went to Zhu for treatment. He was treated three times on the 16th, 18th, and 20th. On the 16th, the illness suddenly worsened, and he died soon after. Cai waited one month and seven days (September 2) and then entrusted a lawyer to send a letter to Zhu, saying that Shunbao's death was caused by Zhu's use of hot medicines such as cinnamon and aconite. He also attached three prescriptions and negotiated with him. Zhu replied that since the letter did not specify how the diagnosis was wrong, how the prescription was inappropriate, or whether the medicines were fatal, he could ask a traditional Chinese medicine organization to judge. Cai then filed a lawsuit. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Wu Zehan opened the Second Criminal Court for questioning. Zhu Ziyun and his lawyer Lu Qi arrived on time, but the bailiff sent the summons to the plaintiff Cai Zirong at No. 26 Yisong Lane and was told that there was no such person. Therefore, he did not arrive. The court gave the prescriptions attached by Cai to Zhu to read. Zhu replied that he could not identify them as his prescriptions because they were not the originals. When asked if he had joined a public association, he replied that he had joined both the China and Shenzhou Medical Associations. Judge Wu stated that the plaintiff's address and other information still needed to be investigated, so he adjourned the hearing to a later date.

Totaling Over Four Thousand Volumes

The Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court, regarding the disposal of various illegal printed materials confiscated in cases endangering the Republic of China, such as books and newspapers, had previously submitted a request to the Ministry of Judicial Administration for permission to burn them. Consequently, since its establishment, the court has held a public burning every three months. The various illegal printed materials confiscated and finalized in cases accumulated within the three months from July 1st to the end of September this year totaled more than eleven kinds. Sent to the Hospital with Detectives Stationed

The property of the Continental Bank at No. 930, Wuding Road, in Huxi, of which No. 14 was rented by Xi Pinshan, who established a morphine manufacturing factory and worked secretly. On the morning of the 16th of this month at 3:00 AM, the factory unexpectedly followed in the footsteps of the morphine factory opened by Cai Bicheng and was also burned down. Xi was unable to extinguish the fire himself and dared not announce the alarm, so he quietly escaped with the workers in the factory. Later, the gatekeeper of the alley discovered the fire and reported it to the Gordon Road Police Station, which dispatched detectives to rush to the scene and cooperate with the fire brigade to put out the fire. The poisons in the house were listed and submitted to the First Special District Local Court for separate confiscation and preservation. This has been reported in the previous newspapers. It is now known that after the fire broke out in the drug manufacturing factory, Wang Nisheng, a 39-year-old worker from Ningbo, was unable to escape with the factory owner Xi Pinshan and others in time, resulting in severe burns to his head, face, hands, and feet. Although he escaped the danger from the flames, he dared not immediately go to the hospital for treatment. He endured the pain and went to hide and recuperate at the home of his fellow villager Wang Sanmao at No. 20 Changzhou Road. Unexpectedly, by noon the next day, his injuries had worsened, and his life was in danger. Wang Sanmao, seeing the situation, did not want him to stay for long and hired a car with his wife, Wang Wangshi, to accompany him to the Tongde Hospital on Tongfu Road. After the doctor treated him and asked about the cause of the burns, Wang Sanmao could not answer, and Wang Nisheng was even more secretive. The hospital became suspicious and notified the police station by telephone, which dispatched detectives to rush to the scene and investigate the injured man. However, he remained vague. The detective then recalled the fire on Wuding Road a few days ago and suspected that he was a worker from that factory, so he went to ask Wang Sanmao and Wang Wangshi whether they knew the injured man's background. According to them, when Wang Nisheng arrived at their house, he claimed to have been burned in a fire on Wuding Road, but they did not know how he had suffered this misfortune. The detective, believing that his guess was correct, transferred Wang Nisheng from Tongde Hospital to the Shanghai Municipal Council Hospital and again questioned him about the cause of his injuries. However, Wang still refused to reveal anything, falsely claiming that he had been burned in a fire in Suzhou and had come to Shanghai for treatment, etc. He still did not know that Wang Sanmao and others had revealed his background, so he made up this lie in the hope of deceiving them. Currently, the police department, because the suspect's injuries are very serious and require treatment, is not conducting a rigorous interrogation, but only dispatched detectives to the hospital to monitor him, waiting for his injuries to heal before thoroughly investigating and sending him to the court for trial.

Supporting Evidence for Monk Yuanzhao Stealing and Selling Property of Longhua Temple 157

Prosecutor Investigates in Detail

To protect the temple property, Abbot Xingkong of Longhua Temple and landowner Lu Mingzhao and others filed a lawsuit in the local court's prosecutor's office against former Abbot Yuanzhao for stealing and selling temple property and appropriating it for his own use, requesting a strict investigation and also attaching civil claims. On the other hand, the Municipal Public Security Bureau apprehended Yuanzhao and recovered a small leather box containing various title deeds, which was transferred to the local court. Prosecutor Wu Deying interrogated him and ordered him to be detained for further investigation. This has been reported in previous newspapers. It is now known that Xingkong and Lu Mingzhao and others thoroughly investigated and discovered that the evil monk Yuanzhao had stolen and sold temple property and embezzled temple funds, amounting to a considerable sum: (1) 37.399 mu of land in Xiaobenqiao, Yitu, 27th Bao, was donated by the Lu family (i.e., Lu Mingzhao's ancestors), with twelve land deeds stored in the temple for safekeeping. In the ninth year of the Republic of China, Yuanzhao received them from Lu Mingzhao and rented them out, but subsequently sold them under false names, pocketing the proceeds. (2) More than 20 mu of land in Litahui and Zhujing, Jinshan County, was purchased by the former abbot Congpei during the 32nd year of the Guangxu reign of the Qing Dynasty and designated as temple property. (3) The Datong area of Lutang, Yitu, 27th Bao (now renamed 890th Tu), was formerly a reed marsh along the coast and was not demarcated into fields, but now it has become fertile land, about 20 mu, which Yuanzhao completely stole and sold to the Jisheng Society. In total, the value of the above-mentioned land is more than 100,000 yuan, all of which was sold by Yuanzhao and appropriated for his own use. It was further found that Yuanzhao had privately purchased properties in the French Concession and opened the Jinshan Cigarette Factory, secretly keeping wives and concubines and having children. Therefore, they reported the results of the investigation to the court for thorough investigation. Yesterday afternoon, Prosecutor Wu Deying ordered Lu Mingzhao and Zhang Liqing, the dibao of 27th Bao (now renamed 890th Tu), to be summoned to the court, and Yuanzhao, who was in custody, was brought in for questioning for a long time. As a result, Yuanzhao was returned to custody to await further instructions.

A Page from the History of Urban Crime 158

A Nine-Year-Old Girl Becomes a Victim

How to Punish Rogues and Prostitutes

丨Transferring Syphilis: Extremely Vicious in Heart, Extremely Foolish in Deed丨

Xiao Lianke, a native of Yangzhou, is 35 years old. He used to work in the local police station and has been unemployed recently. He lives at No. 124 Pingjili Road in the French Concession with his wife, Zhang, 33 years old, and his daughter, Laixi, 9 years old. Xiao has an older sister, Fan Xiaoshi, who currently lives in the spare room of the home of Bian Shouan (48 years old), a fellow villager, at No. 222 Shengjili Kou, Mintini Yin Road. Bian Shouan and his wife, Bian Yushi, 45 years old, used to run a brothel at No. 4 Shengjili. Recently, due to the French police's crackdown on brothels, the Bian couple stopped their business because it was unprofitable and moved to No. 222 Shengjili Kou. Bian has a son named Yukang, also known as Xiao Anzi, 17 years old, who has not yet learned a trade and roams around every day. He is of bad character and recently became involved with a young prostitute, Zhang Xiaoxizi, 15 years old, from Rugao. Because the prostitute suffers from syphilitic sores, Bian Yukang contracted syphilis. Bian immediately argued with the prostitute, Zhang Xiaoxizi, who replied to Bian Yukang, "Don't worry, if you can rape a virgin, the poison in your body can be transferred to her, and your body can be restored to its original state." From then on, Bian and the prostitute Zhang were looking for a virgin in the hope of getting rid of the disease. Unexpectedly, Xiao Lianke's daughter, Laixi, went to play at her aunt Fan Xiaoshi's house on the afternoon of the 16th of this month around 7:00 PM. At that time, the girl's aunt, Xiaoshi, and Bian Shouan and Bian Yushi were all out on business. Only Bian's son, Yukang, was at home. At this time, the prostitute Zhang Xiaoxizi also went to Bian's house to chat with Yukang. Seeing Laixi nearby, she immediately instigated Yukang to commit bestiality. With Zhang Buxizi's help, they first pressed Laixi down on a wicker chair, pulled off her small clothes, and ordered Yukang to rape her. At that time, Laixi was young and weak and unable to resist, so she had to submit to their will and was defiled. After the act, Zhang and Bian Yukang threatened Laixi not to speak out. The girl was ignorant and endured in silence. After the act, the girl did not feel any pain until the next day when the girl's mother, Xiao Zhangshi, washed her daughter's clothes and saw stains on her pants. At first, she did not think it was strange, but when she washed the girl's clothes for the second time and saw blood stains on her pants, just like before, she paid attention and observed Laixi's actions for the past few days and felt that something was wrong. She then questioned the girl strictly, and the girl, unable to hide anything, told her mother everything. The Xiao couple were shocked and reported the incident to the French police station the day before yesterday. Detective Liu Songtian went to arrest Bian Yukang and the prostitute Zhang. After questioning by the police chief, Bian and others admitted to the rape. The police chief then ordered the girl to be sent to Guangci Hospital. The doctor examined her and found that Laixi had not only been injured by the rape but also contracted venereal disease, which had risen to her abdomen and was very serious. Based on the hospital's diagnosis, the police station sent the defendants to the Special Second Court for trial today.

Zhabei Businessmen Jointly Guarantee Zheng Tingfu 160

Hundreds of Businesses Come Out to Jointly Guarantee

Saying It is Reactionary is Extremely Bizarre

After Zheng Tingfu, the owner of the Xin Kang Chemical Factory on Gonghe New Road, Hongnanshan, Zhabei, was arrested, various circles requested his release, but it has not been approved. Hundreds of businesses in the Zhabei district, such as Shunxin Lianyou, Sanmao, Ruitai, and Changrentai, jointly submitted a petition to the Central Party Department and the Municipal Government yesterday, requesting the Public Security Bureau to release him. The original petition stated, "Presenting a petition for the arrest of a good citizen, lamenting the closing of the Yuanmen, daring to directly state, humbly requesting that you quickly order the Public Security Bureau to release him. We businessmen have been operating in Zhabei for many years, acting cautiously and responsibly, and have never heard of any other situations. Now, regarding Zheng Tingfu, the owner of the Xin Kang Pharmaceutical Factory, he is filial to his parents, treats people kindly, and has never been heard to have any private party affiliations or ambiguous behavior. His reputation for loyalty and integrity is well known, and his name for not being obsequious is known to us businessmen. Today, he was suddenly arrested, claiming to have reactionary suspicions. We businessmen were shocked and terrified upon hearing the news. If Zheng Tingfu is truly as you say, with his bad deeds clearly visible, then let him be executed and punished, and he will die without regret. Calamity and blessings have no door, and destruction is self-inflicted. We businessmen also definitely do not want to aid the wicked, causing harm to society and danger to the country. However, there are things that we cannot remain silent about. Zheng Tingfu is neither a cunning and scheming person nor a desperate and lawless person. Observing his research in the chemical industry, he has spent more than 20 years, exhausting his efforts and sparing no effort. He established a factory in Hongnanshan, Zhabei, and has been there for 13 years. His business aspirations truly have a spirit of perseverance, which has led him to become a figure respected by everyone in the business community today. We businessmen are neither old friends nor close friends, but we are in close proximity and have more accurate knowledge. In ordinary times, we have never seen the slightest flaw. Now, suddenly he is said to have reactionary suspicions, which is extremely bizarre. At this time of national turmoil, it is the time for villains to cast shadows on others. Even famous scholars cannot escape slander. How can a mere businessman bear this? Thinking of Your Departments and Government as the protectors of our people, if Zheng Yanfu's strange injustice is only slightly illuminated by the candor of truth and falsehood, we are deeply afraid that the forging within will destroy the bones and tails. Therefore, we businessmen dare to prove his usual behavior and especially jointly appeal to Your Departments and Government to quickly order the Municipal Public Security Bureau to release him in order to maintain goodness and secure business, then we will be grateful beyond measure. We respectfully present this petition."

Shanghai Municipal Council Fire Department Report 161

The Shanghai Municipal Council Fire Department Director's report for September states that a total of 56 alarms were received during the month, of which ten were false alarms. The property endangered by the fire was 1,264,055 yuan within the concession and 468,000 yuan in the special donation area. The actual losses were 16,010 yuan and 1,380 yuan respectively. Three people died due to special hazardous incidents, and sixteen people were injured due to fire alarms and hazardous incidents. One firefighter was injured.

The Emergency Squad ambulance received 380 alarms, and as a result, 392 injured and sick people were sent to the hospital. The Medical Squad ambulance transported 206 patients. 1934, 10, 19

Impersonating Public Officials to Collect Stall Donations 162

Zhang Yinsheng and others identify Chen Agen

Mao Quanzhong, a staff member of the Yimiao Police Station in the city, was patrolling Fuyou Road at 10:00 AM yesterday when he saw two vegetable stalls obstructing traffic and ordered them to close. Unexpectedly, the stall vendors, named Zhang Yinsheng (43 years old, from Jiangyin) and Zhao Dean (29 years old, from Ningbo, residing at No. 2 Hengdeli, Fuyou Road), claimed that they paid a monthly stall donation of $1.20 and were not in violation of regulations. Staff member Mao immediately asked to see the receipt, and they claimed that the stall donation was paid to Chen Agen, who was acting as a public official, and insured by Chen, so there was no receipt. Believing that the case involved the private collection of stall donations, he took the two stall vendors to the police station for verification. According to the defendant's confession, Chen Agen lived at No. 1 Ruyili, Wutong Alley. Director Liu immediately sent the police to bring Chen Agen to the station. Chen, who claimed to be a 27-year-old fish vendor from Ningbo, denied collecting the donations. However, the two stall vendors, Zhang and Zhao, identified him as the one to whom they had paid the money in person. The case involves impersonating a public official, collecting donations from stall vendors without authorization, and is suspected of deception and fraud to obtain wealth. It has been ordered to be transferred to the Public Security Bureau for legal proceedings.

Spring and Autumn

Little Western Paradise 173

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Third 回: Unresolved, Zero Peek Door, Pity for the Girl, Willing to Hear Hardships, Cherishing Jade, Visiting a Poor Family

On the flat ground, there was a rectangular earthen platform. That was the sleeping pit. Some wooden stakes were nailed to the earthen wall, and a few large and small holes were dug. Their family's boxes and cabinets were all there. Poor people are really poor to this extent. I think that is no different from a dead body lying on the ground. Your Little Western Paradise is a place frequented by wealthy people. It seems that although we are not wealthy, if you told me to live in a cave, I would not do it either. Why do you want to make caves? The tea house boy pouted his mouth toward the back of the house and laughed, "The caves are in the backyard. You can go and see them." They are all caves, but there is a big difference between good and bad. Cheng Zhiqian laughed, "I want to see how good they are." Saying this, he left this small courtyard and walked toward the large courtyard behind. Here, there was an old house being demolished, leaving only a little of its skeleton. Lime and hemp ropes were piled up inside, as well as the tools used by the craftsmen. Passing through this old house, there were two or three courtyards of newly built houses that had not yet been completed. Eight hundred and ten carpenters and masons were all out of work, gathered in the courtyard. Cheng Zhiqian thought to himself, could there be some problem? So he walked closer to take a look. By the time he entered this courtyard, it turned out that the workers were having a meal. Observing it, there was a special scene. They were in piles of three, groups of five, either sitting around the edge of the stone steps or sitting against the wall in a straight line. They were all covered in mud and ash, so they could not be considered clean, so everyone was sitting on the ground. In the midst of all these people, there was a large wicker basket filled with fist-sized cold black buns. Next to the basket was a wooden bucket with a lid, filled with a bucket of water. It looked like it was hot, but it was not boiled water, because the workers were seen drinking the water very casually, not as if it was scalding their mouths. There were also dozens of earthenware bowls and a basket of chopsticks. When the workers came, they took a bowl and a pair of chopsticks. Then the hand holding the chopsticks took a piece of black bun from the basket. As for the earthenware bowl, it was used to scoop more than half a bowl of water from the bucket. (44)

On Mother Guo's Affairs 174

— Zhao Shaokuang

Men of extraordinary talent and character are often established through the teachings of virtuous mothers. This is true in ancient and modern times, both in China and abroad. In recent times, many virtuous leaders of the party and the country, and prominent figures in society, have followed their mother's teachings, strived to achieve their ambitions, and created great careers. In the autumn of the twenty-third year of the Republic of China, I first met Mr. Guo Jianying at sea and deeply admired his dignity and composure, which were unlike ordinary people. After a conversation, I learned the details of his mother's life. I respectfully said: The sacred and beautiful virtues of Madam Tai are worthy of being passed down! According to: Madam Tai's surname is Xiao, the eighth daughter of Mr. Xiao Minji of Southern Guangdong. Mr. Xiao lived in Honolulu and started his career in trade. Although he accumulated a great fortune, Madam Tai was frugal and restrained her desires, never confined by extravagant habits. At the age of eighteen, she married Mr. Guo Ronghui. The following year, she gave birth to Mr. Jianying. A year later, Mr. Guo passed away. Madam Tai became a widow and was so grief-stricken that she did not want to live. At that time, Mr. Guo's parents were still healthy. Madam Tai piously served her esteemed elders, diligently raised her orphaned son, never disobeying or neglecting, teaching and nurturing him, and became a model for women in the village, praised by everyone. After her parents-in-law passed away, Madam Tai supervised Mr. Jianying's education even more vigorously. Madam Tai was from Zhongshan and had heard much about Mr. Sun Yat-sen, a great man of his generation, whose love of learning in his youth and diligence in his adulthood were due to a good family education. Therefore, she constantly instructed Mr. Jianying, saying: "Your father passed away early. You should strive to study hard and inherit your father's legacy." She further said: "When you have completed your studies and put them to use in the future, serving society, you should make serving the motherland your primary goal, and do not be content with personal wealth and comfort." When Mr. Jianying completed his studies, he traveled to Australia to engage in trade. He was unwilling to become a wealthy merchant and was always concerned about national affairs, thinking of emulating Bu Shi's contribution to the border. If not for Madam Tai's past diligent teachings, how could he have achieved this? In the autumn of the twenty-second year, Mr. Jianying, realizing that the national crisis was becoming increasingly urgent, did not have time to live in peace. He traveled across the ocean to conduct foreign publicity and raise funds for emergency relief. At that time, Madam Tai died of illness in her village. Mr. Jianying has been grieving ever since for not being able to care for her until the end of her life. Alas! Madam Tai's expectations of Mr. Jianying were only to be public-minded and forget private interests, to be concerned about the country and forget the family. Now that Mr. Jianying is able to worry about the country as if he were hungry and thirsty, I know that Madam Tai will be smiling in the afterlife. What else could she regret? Madam Tai was born in the thirty-second year before the founding of the Republic of China and lived to the age of fifty-four. She had a son, Jianying, two grandsons, and one granddaughter.

Odds and Ends 175

(Yan Zi) 176

I wish I had no love, I fear love like I fear debt.

Taking away my peace, there is only love and debt. If a person does not have these two things, the world he has can be happy.

There he saw all the things of the Golden Age, freedom, equality. He drinks, he eats, he is at peace. He is not afraid of women, not afraid of anything!

Reading Notes 177

— Xu Bibo

In recent years, the sound of change, change has made a lot of noise. No matter what field you are in, if there is no new reform, people are gathering there to discuss, "He is behind the times." Even when it comes to literature and art, Classical Chinese is indeed outdated to the extreme, and even the use of Vernacular Chinese, there are many gentlemen who like change, clamoring to use Popular Language to overthrow it. I can't help but think of the outdated and outdated proverb poem, "The waves of the Yangtze River urge the waves ahead, new people in the world replace old people," using a sentence or two to compare with the current situation, I really feel a lot of emotion!

However, no matter what, if it has its own indelible true value, no matter how it changes, there will always be someone who can express sympathy for it. Just like Classical Chinese, although some people think it is outdated, there are others who think it is a national treasure and always maintain a spirit of support, so that it is not completely buried.

The current martial arts novels are certainly also being eliminated. People who are generally overcorrecting directly regard the two words "martial arts" as poisonous snakes and fierce beasts. Therefore, the spirit of the people is gradually declining, and it has become a cowardly habit of "non-resistance." This really makes people with good intentions feel short of breath!

My friend Gu Mingdao, because of illness in his feet, had to retire to his hometown and devote himself to writing. At first, he used the "Tidujuan Record," which earned people's tears, to win the welcome of the world, but he was too accustomed to decadence. So he shifted his magnificent style and changed to writing long works of "patriotic," "revolutionary," and "martial arts" genres, especially "Wild River Female Knight" was the most popular. Because this novel mixes the above three kinds of consciousness, depicting a prostitute female knight Fang Yuqin, like a raging fire, simply makes people want to forget to eat and sleep after reading his works. Youlian Film Company also explored and produced the film, which is even more popular in the world, complementing each other. Now his fourth giant work is meeting the world again. He entrusted the Samsung Bookstore, which published this book, to send me a copy. After reading it, I feel that it is carrying on from the past and opening up to the future, with wonderful ideas arising in a loop. And writing about Yuqin's lively and vibrant posture is really enough to make people feel leisurely and distant.

Desolate Moonlight 178

— Dongsheng

Imperial Incense Drifting Record 179

— Original by Princess Deling of Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

In this enormous green gauze tent, there is enough space to hide a huge number of cavalry: not to mention that people's bodies will never be seen by outsiders, even the horses' feet will absolutely not be exposed.

At this time, the area we were passing through was very desolate. There were no grand or numerous buildings on either side of the tracks: only piles of scattered low houses, covered with broken tiles, mostly the nests of poor people, sheltering them from wind and rain. There were also some wild or domesticated beasts, such as cattle, sheep, horses, pigs, deer, etc., moving about in the fields: some of them immersed their entire bodies in those filthy little rivers, getting completely covered in mud, which was also quite laughable. The Empress Dowager usually liked birds and beasts very much. Now that she saw them jumping freely in the wild, she was of course particularly interested. Unfortunately, among the people she brought, from the accompanying ministers down to the little eunuchs, there was no one who had a special knowledge of zoology, otherwise she would definitely have reused them immediately.

In Guanwai, since it is generally also within Chinese territory, then there is one thing that is naturally indispensable! That is, many mounds full of fields, the graves of dead people. The Chinese people's lack of understanding of economic principles in the use of land is everywhere; but in Guanwai, the wild grass seems to grow more luxuriantly than in Guannei, so each tomb has a green and oily grass mat spread over it, which looks relatively beautiful! There are no high mountains rising here. On the horizon, there are only these mounds. (154)

Lanzhou Fruit Vendors 180

— (Cheng Zhao)

Lanzhou is located on the banks of the Yellow River, with fertile soil and convenient irrigation. Therefore, in addition to growing wheat and grains, most residents take growing melons, fruits, tea, and vegetables as their "only" sideline business.

Every evening, in the quiet river under the hazy moonlight, the fruit vendors leisurely row their small boats to the villages to sell the goods for the next day. While "yanking" the oars, they also hum a "little tune," which is quite exciting and flavorful.

When the sky has not yet revealed the whiteness of the fish's belly, the fruit vendors have already rowed their heavy boats back, busily washing the "new goods" in preparation for the early market.

Lanzhou's special famous fruits include several kinds such as apples, pears, persimmons, "stupid eggs" (a local fruit), and sand fruits. Watermelons and cucumbers are rare.

Every day, the money earned by fruit vendors is about two or three yuan, which is enough for a family's expenses! So the life of Lanzhou fruit vendors is really very affluent.

Random Talk

More on Opening Remarks 181

— Xun Zi

After reading Mr. Zhang Zhenlü's "On Opening Remarks," many unsystematic thoughts floated into my mind!

Since the popularity of wireless radio, every household, with great effort, has been constantly filled with the sounds of stringed instruments. Storytellers, thanks to the blessings of material civilization, have had a good run of business. The opening remarks, as an accessory, have also become fashionable. Last year, I compiled "The Green Butterfly Double Ballad" for Zhao Hesun and "The Imperial Stele Pavilion Ballad" for Zhu Yaoxiang and Zhao Jiaqiu. Thus, I began to correspond with storytellers, who then requested me to write opening remarks. I couldn't help but respond with a few pieces. In reality, this "toy" is not easy to deal with. If it's too profound or too elegant, the listeners won't understand. If it's too crude or shallow, it becomes like the Eastern Village tune, making people's hairs stand on end. The ballad singer Qi Lianfang told me that Mr. Mao Zijian enjoyed listening to stories but rarely approved of the opening remarks written by contemporaries. He only praised the opening remarks written by Mr. Qi Fanniu and myself, saying they were both elegant and popular. In fact, Mr. Qi, as a literary figure and a member of the Guangyu Society, had poetic fame in his youth. Now, in his old age, he uses his remaining energy to do these playful writings. His works, which can be called "domestic treasures", are naturally extraordinary. As for me, I just scribble them down when I'm in a good mood, without caring about the skillfulness. I'm afraid I've failed Mr. Mao Zijian's praise!

There is a ballad singer who can write his own opening remarks. Regardless of whether they are well-written or not, he can still be considered outstanding among the mediocre! When his father died, he composed an opening remark mourning his father, which became very popular. Radio stations played it almost every day. However, upon closer examination, it's simply not a good example! Throughout history, how many poets and lyricists have we seen include poems or lyrics mourning a father in their collections? Because the immeasurable depth of parental kindness cannot be described with words. In ancient times, people could compose poems on high ground, writing about mountains and rivers, or the two capitals, but we never heard of anyone writing about the universe. The ancients had a saying: "Extreme sorrow has no words." When the one who gave us life passes away, we are too busy crying and longing for them to have the mood to search for phrases and compose music. However, having said that, in this day and age, knowing how to "gain a reputation for filial piety" is still considered gentlemanly. It is already extremely rare for fashionable people not to follow Chen Duxiu in shouting the slogan "Of all evils, filial piety is the greatest"!

Zhu Yaoxiang published a collection of opening remarks called "Joy in Books," half of which were old opening remarks from manuscripts, and half of which were new works sent to him by listeners outside of Shanghai after he broadcasted on the radio. Because he was afraid that there might be inappropriate content, he asked me to revise a portion of it. I believe that although this "toy" is a minor skill, those without considerable cultivation in classical poetry should not even think of dealing with it! Because the tones are actually natural rhythms, and opening remarks, like classical poetry, must pay attention to tones. As for the rhyming parts, although "Dong Dong" and "Jiang Yang" are commonly used interchangeably, one must follow the Suzhou dialect. For example, although "shi" (時) and "li" (離) both belong to the fourth branch, it is best to avoid using them in opening remarks! It can be seen that even this small "toy" has rules and regulations, which cannot be imitated by those who casually start writing!

Storytellers are very good at taking shortcuts. A few days ago, I saw that Zhu Yaoxiang had taken a segment from the Imperial Stele Pavilion, which I wrote for him, where Meng Yuehua and Wang Youdao's younger sister tease each other, and turned it into an opening remark called "Sister-in-law Teasing," which was published in the News Evening Post. Also, an opening remark about Chen Sufen's love death that was published in a small newspaper was clearly written by me, but the storyteller who liked it wrote his name on it and claimed it as his work. It's truly a case of eating and forgetting who grew the rice! However, appropriating someone else's work as one's own, when facing one's conscience, I'm afraid one can't help but feel ashamed, right?

Correspondence 182

To the esteemed editor of the "Chun Qiu" section:

Regarding the postscript in your newspaper's "The Fragrant Incense Misty Records" from October 4th, "Yesterday, I was informed by Mr. Yi that according to the Qing Dynasty regulations, only high-ranking Manchu officials could use the term 'slave,' so Yuan Shikai should have referred to himself as '臣' (subject) when meeting with Empress Dowager Cixi," I, during the late Qing Dynasty, worked in the office of Jiangbei Governor-General Wang Shizhen. I saw that his memorials referred to himself as "slave," and Wang was from Zhengding Prefecture, not a Manchu bannerman. At the time, I was also suspicious of this. Later, I consulted with Xu Yusheng, a document specialist, who said that all Han Chinese military officials who were qualified to submit memorials directly could refer to themselves as "slave." When Yuan Shikai was in charge of the six towns of the Beiyang Army, he referred to himself as "slave" when meeting with the Empress Dowager. This may have been permitted by Qing Dynasty regulations. Today, people are ashamed to call themselves "slave," but back then, it was an honor. I offer what I have heard for your reference and respectfully request Mr. Yi's guidance.

With best wishes,

Yan Zhongwen respectfully.

Education News

Ministry of Education Approves University Staff Pension 183

Regulations have been promulgated... Qinghua and Beijing Normal University staff now receive pensions

After the National Government promulgated the Regulations on Pensions and Bereavement Allowances for School Staff and Teachers in previous years, there have been some requests for bereavement allowances. However, there have not been many requests for pensions. Although there are not many teachers who are over sixty years old and have worked in schools for fifteen consecutive years, some may have been discouraged from applying due to financial difficulties in education, administrative inabilities, or fear that the process would be difficult. However, since the government has established regulations, there will eventually be a day when they are universally implemented. The implementation of this pension system is a great comfort to those who have served diligently in the field of education and is welcomed by educators nationwide. It has been learned that the Ministry of Education issued certificates in July (previously approved by the Executive Yuan and then by the National Government for record) to those who are entitled to pensions. One such person is Wang Lianxi, a staff member of National Tsinghua University, who has served for more than ten years and is over sixty years old. He will receive an annual pension of 504 yuan starting from his retirement. Recently, the pension of Wang Xin, a staff member of Beijing Normal University, was also approved for an annual payment of 210 yuan (having served for more than fifteen years but less than twenty years). The Ministry of Education has submitted the situation to the Executive Yuan for approval and referral to the National Government for record. The original text of the pension regulations (promulgated by the National Government) is very long. The following are excerpts of several key points:

Regulations on Pensions and Bereavement Allowances for School Staff and Teachers (Bereavement Allowance Section Omitted)

(1) Any staff or teacher who has served continuously for more than fifteen years and is over sixty years old may apply for retirement or be requested to retire by the school and receive a pension. Those who are under sixty years old but are physically weak and unable to perform their duties may also receive a pension, but only if they do not hold other positions. (1) If a staff or teacher is injured on duty, resulting in disability and inability to perform their duties, they may receive a pension even if they have not reached the age limit in the previous article, but only if they do not hold other positions. (1) The pension for part-time teachers shall be 20% of the average annual salary of the last three years. (1) The pension standard shall be determined separately according to the final monthly salary and years of service. (1) For those with a final monthly salary of 200 yuan, (the word "final" is omitted below) the annual pension is 900 yuan for those with fifteen years or more but less than twenty years of service. (The following will be abbreviated, using "and" to connect the years of service and the amount in yuan) 1050 yuan for twenty years or more but less than twenty-five years of service, (The following will be abbreviated, using "and" to connect the years of service and the amount in yuan) 1200 yuan for twenty-five years or more. (2) For those with a monthly salary of 150 yuan or more but less than 200 yuan, 735 yuan, 840 yuan, and 945 yuan. (3) For those with a monthly salary of 120 yuan or more (omitting "less than 150 yuan" and similar phrases below), 64 yuan, 729 yuan, and 810 yuan. (4) For those with a monthly salary of 100 yuan or more, 594 yuan, 660 yuan, and 726 yuan. (5) For those with a monthly salary of 80 yuan or more, 540 yuan, 594 yuan, and 648 yuan. (6) For those with a monthly salary of 60 yuan or more, 462 yuan, 504 yuan, and 546 yuan. (7) For those with a monthly salary of 45 yuan or more, 381 yuan, 413 yuan, and 445 yuan. (8) For those with a monthly salary of 30 yuan or more, 296 yuan, 219 yuan, and 342 yuan. (9) For those with a monthly salary of 20 yuan or more, 210 yuan, 225 yuan, and 245 yuan. (10) For those with a monthly salary of less than 20 yuan, 180 yuan, 192 yuan, and 204 yuan. (The pension for staff and full-time teachers shall be granted 30% of the final annual salary in addition to the above standards. The pension for part-time teachers shall be 30% of the average annual salary of the last three years.) (1) National schools shall have pensions paid by the national treasury, provincial schools by the provincial treasury, municipal and county district schools by the municipal and county district education funds, and private schools shall consider their financial situation and provide payments at their discretion. (1) Applicants for pensions should provide a resume of facts and the amount of fees requested, and the school principal should submit it to the competent educational administrative agency for approval.

Jiangsu Provincial Secondary School Teachers' Association Held Meeting Yesterday 186

(Suzhou, 19th) The 15th Congress of Representatives of the Jiangsu Provincial Secondary School Teachers' Association was held in Suzhou today. Thirty-one representatives from various schools attended. Chen Zhenbai presided over the meeting. The following important cases were discussed and resolved: (1) After the county normal school is closed, the provincial normal school should be expanded to popularize national education; (2) It is requested that the Ministry of Education issue a weekly work schedule plan for high school and junior high school students; (3) It is decided that the educational department should start organizing normal school entrance examinations this year, and the minimum standards for teaching materials for each subject should be promulgated as soon as possible; (4) It is requested that the educational department restore direct promotion from junior high school as an incentive; (5) It is requested that the educational department increase the school budget for the 24th year to implement specialized positions and implement seniority-based salary increases; (6) It is requested that the educational department revise the free education policy for the children of service personnel in provincial educational institutions; (7) It is requested that the educational department amend the newly established regulations restricting the protection of teachers and staff; (8) It is requested that the educational department compile the salary standards for teachers and staff in provincial schools, etc. After the meeting, the four schools of Suzhou Middle School, Suzhou Agricultural School, Suzhou Industrial School, and Suzhou Women's Normal School held a public banquet at the New Suzhou Hotel. Thirteen schools have been rated as D and will be reprimanded, including Guoji, Huaxia, St. Paul, Anshun, Jinrong, Dahua, Ningbo Fellow Villagers Association, the 3rd, 6th, and 7th Schools, the Second Elementary School of the Charity Group, Shuye Chongde, and Xuanmin. In addition, Sixing Private Elementary School has not improved after being reprimanded by the bureau and has been rated as D. The bureau has reported to the municipal government to revoke its registration.

Sports News

The Third Municipal Middle School Joint Sports Meet 193

To be held at Jiaotong University for three days starting on the 8th of next month.

Registration starts today and ends on the 27th.

The third municipal middle school joint sports meet is scheduled to be held at National Jiaotong University from November 8th to 10th. All materials for this year's sports meet drill, competition guidelines, registration forms, the sports meet song, and regulations for participation in track and field events by secondary physical education schools have been stipulated. The Education Bureau will distribute these to each school, and registration forms, specifying the sports to be entered and the athletes selected, must be properly submitted to the temporary office at the Municipal First Public Gymnasium on Daji Road in the Southern City by the 27th of this month for arrangement. The various rules are recorded as follows:

Competition Guidelines (1) Male and female athletes are generally divided into Group A and Group B. The standards are as follows: Male Group A: Weight of 50 kilograms or more, height of 1.6 meters or more. Any athlete meeting either of these standards is considered Group A. Male Group B: All those who do not meet the Group A standards are classified as Group B. Female Group A: Weight of 45 kilograms or more. Female Group B: Weight less than 45 kilograms. (2) Female athletes in Group B must have their weight re-weighed before participating in each sports competition, and male athletes in Group B must also have their height re-measured. (3) When the number of participants in a sports competition is too large to compete at once, preliminary and semi-final rounds should be held before the finals. (4) There must be at least six athletes in the finals, unless this is not possible in reality. (5) At least two athletes should be selected from each group in the preliminary and semi-final rounds. (6) All athletes must affix two designated numbers (matching those specified on the order sheet), one on the chest and one on the back. (7) Athletes who have already forfeited their right to compete may not re-enter the competition. (8) Athletes who engage in immoral behavior on the field will be immediately disqualified. (9) Track athletes who intentionally push, shove, or run diagonally to obstruct the progress of others will be disqualified, regardless of whether it occurs in the preliminary, semi-final, or final rounds. (10) Athletes may not use instruments or other strong stimulants to enhance their performance and seek victory during competitions. (11) If athletes have protests, they must submit them in writing to the judging committee for review and decision within one hour of the occurrence. (12) The protest letter must be signed and sealed by the physical education teacher and the administrative person in charge of the athlete's school. (13) The decision of the judging committee on the protest letter is final and cannot be protested again. (14) The athletes' clothing is to be designed by each school itself and must be clean and elegant. (15) The order of competition for each event will be drawn by the organizers of the event. (16) Athletes in field events should attempt their jumps or throws in the order determined by the organizers. (17) Field event athletes who are also participating in track events may be allowed by the track and field referees to attempt their jumps or throws out of order. (18) The starting positions or running lanes for track athletes will be determined by drawing lots. (19) If there are identical scores in any competition, the tied athletes will compete in another round of competition, jump or throw again, raise or lower the bar until a winner is determined.

Participation of Physical Education Schools. Regulations for participation in the third municipal middle school joint sports meet by private secondary physical education schools: (1) These regulations are formulated in accordance with Article 12 of the regulations of the Second Shanghai Municipal Middle School Joint Sports Meet. (2) All private secondary physical education schools in this city may participate in various sports of the Third Shanghai Municipal Middle School Joint Sports Meet. (3) Sports are divided into two parts: group exercises and track and field. The events are as follows: A. Group Exercises: 1. Grand Exercises: Each school should send one-tenth of its students as representatives to participate. 2. Group Exercises: Such as Chinese martial arts, walking exercises, calisthenics, and dance. Each school is limited to two sections. B. Track and Field: 1. Boys: i. Field Events: High jump, long jump, shot put, pole vault, discus throw, javelin throw. ii. Track Events: 100 meters, 200 meters, 400 meters, 800 meters, 1500 meters, 110-meter hurdles, 800-meter relay, 1600-meter relay. 2. Girls: i. Field Events: High jump, long jump, shot put, javelin throw. ii. Track Events: 50 meters, 100 meters, 200 meters, 400-meter relay. The above track and field events for both boys and girls are divided into Group A and Group B. The standards for grouping are found in the "Athlete Selection Guidelines." (4) Participation in Sports Events: 1. Each athlete can register for a maximum of four field events for boys and three for girls. 2. Each school can send a maximum of four athletes per group in each event. (5) No championships will be awarded for participation in each sports event; awards will be given to the best performers. (6) Certificates will be awarded to those with excellent performance in group exercises.

Sports Meet Song: What is today? We, the youth, must shoulder the Party and the nation with iron shoulders. Endure hardship and strive for improvement, forged a hundred times. Joint skill demonstration is no accident. Boost morale, group performance, be neat, lively, and comprehensive. Peace and struggle, unyielding and indomitable. Track and field competitions, strive to be the first. Everyone cheers, the city's middle school students are actively capable and heroic. Everyone swears to use these good skills to face difficulties and be pioneers.

Group Exercises Teaching Materials: Section 1: Limb Exercises. 1. Step to the side with the foot, raise both arms to the side. 2. Raise heels, raise both arms upward to the side. 3. Return to position 1. 4. Return left foot and both arms. 5, 6, 7, 8: Repeat the same for the right foot. Do this for a total of thirty-two beats. Section 2: Chest Raising Exercise. 1. Raise both arms straight forward. 2. Extend both arms to the left and right, palms facing up, and raise the chest at the same time. 3. Return to position 1. 4. Return both arms. 5, 6, 7, 8: Repeat the same. Do this for a total of thirty-two beats. Section 3: 1. Jump with feet apart, arms bent at sides. 2. Bend the upper body forward, extending arms forward (downward). 3. Return to position 1. 4. Return to original position. 5, 6, 7, 8: Perform as described above until the 32nd beat. Section 4: Body Rotation Exercise. Preparation: Stand with feet apart, make a fist, bend elbows horizontally at the waist, making a fist-holding posture, upper arms vertical. 1. Rotate the upper body to the left, punching the right fist to the left (arm horizontal). 2. Return the upper body to the center, retracting the right fist. 3. Rotate the upper body to the right, punching the left fist to the right. 4. Return the upper body to the center, retracting the left fist. 5, 6, 7, 8: Repeat the same. Do this for a total of thirty-two beats, until returning to the standing position on the last beat. Section 5: Waist Exercise. 1. Hands on hips, left foot in a left lunge. 2. Lean the upper body to the left. 3. Return the upper body upright. 4. Retract to the left and right, put down hands. 5. Hands on hips, right foot in a right lunge. 6. Lean the upper body to the right. 7. Return the upper body upright. 8. Retract the right foot. Do this for a total of thirty-two beats. Section 6: Rapid Exercise. 1. Jump with feet apart and raise both arms to the side horizontally. 2. Return arms to the original position. Repeat for a total of thirty-two beats. Section 7: Breathing Exercise. 1-2: Raise arms upward from the front, inhale. 3-4: Lower arms downward from the side, exhale. 5, 6, 7, 8: Repeat the same. Do this for a total of sixteen beats.

Commercial News

Yesterday's Financial Situation Was Very Different From the Previous Day; Speculative Premiums Fell by 31 Yuan 201

News of Suppression Arose, Buyers Began to Emerge

The gold market, which had been rising sharply for days, fell yesterday due to the stabilization of public sentiment. This was a normal phenomenon after a continuous rise. Many parties sold off, and there was still a large amount of pressure in the market. At the same time, rumors far from the truth were spreading. Early in the morning, the overseas silver market saw continued declines in both England and the United States, exchange rates rose uniformly, and the price of gold in London fell by six pence. Reports in newspapers that the Ministry of Finance and the banking industry were doing their best to suppress the gold market and use balancing forces were numerous. In addition, rumors that the market price quoted by the Central Bank would be supplied as much as possible, etc., made people feel exhausted. In fact, after a sharp rise in speculative trading, a reversal was inevitable. It was also reported that there had been transactions at 980 yuan in the night market, causing the market to anticipate a drop. The initial calls were for 890 yuan, but there were no transactions, and the situation was chaotic. The depletion of chips in the market was very obvious. It immediately rebounded to over 1,000 yuan. After the opening, although it fell due to the news that the market price quoted by the Central Bank was level in England but up 0.0625 in the United States, the tariff fell by six percent, and the standard speculative premium was fixed at 985 yuan and a half, trading was still active but without a market. People became agitated again. Although the foreign exchange market was loose, it was not much, and the short sellers in the market covered again, gradually pulling the price up. The appetites of banks varied, but the foreign exchange market was trending towards tightening. Public sentiment was still stable, and the price rose to 1,008 yuan. Afterwards, the Guangdong banks began to sell off, and the price of gold softened, but it still struggled around the 1,000 yuan mark. When unfavorable news, such as the preparation of huge amounts of drafts and the joint suppression of the foreign exchange market by three banks, resurfaced, the Guangdong banks continued to maintain their downward pressure. Thereafter, sellers emerged slightly, and a downward trend began, but there was much hesitation along the way. As the foreign exchange market hardened, with the exchange rate for British currency at 1.4 and the exchange rate for US currency at 33.0625 yuan, the price retreated to within 990 yuan, falling by nearly twenty yuan. However, the overall trend was still flat, and it stabilized after the low, with the price of gold gradually rising again. This was because chips were still scarce and there were no sellers. The market was initially stable but then weakened. Large investors' desire to sell resurfaced, and the foreign exchange market also became loose and flooded, so the market situation weakened. General buyers waited patiently for the opportunity, so the pressure began to take effect. However, there was still much struggle after the low. Later, the domestic market became even harder, once retreating into the 80-yuan range. Buyers became active when the price was low, and the selling pressure disappeared again at this point. The market rebounded significantly before closing. The turbulence throughout the day was still great, but it was not as severe as in the previous days. This was also a common phenomenon. Small short positions at low prices were mostly squeezed, so the overall trend turned weak. There were no large sellers in the market, and the extremely large short position of Tongfeng Yong was also unexpected and worthy of attention. The market situation for the day is recorded below:

The market opened at 1,000 yuan, down 17 yuan from the previous close. Yuanchun sold off smoothly, retreating from 1,001 yuan to 996 yuan. The Central Bank's quoted price was level for British currency but up 0.0625 for US currency, and the tariff was down six percent. However, Zhengchang, Wanxing, Hengyu, and Yongheng still bought on the dip, pushing the price up to 1,004 yuan. Dafa and Yongshun Mao sold off. At this time, the market situation was softer, with supply exceeding demand, and it retreated to 998.5 yuan. After all, the Central Bank's quoted price had no buying or selling, and public sentiment was still good. Yuqing, Yongshen, and Changyong bought off one after another, and the price rose to 1,007.7 yuan. Hongli, Qingyu, Fuxing Yong, etc., sold off, gradually retreating to within 2 yuan. Bingxing, Hengyu, Fuxing Yong suddenly came in to buy, and the price rose to 8 yuan. Dingkang, Dadecheng, Yifeng Yong sold off, retreating to 2 yuan. At this time, because the HSBC Bank's quoted prices for British and American currency did not move, public sentiment stabilized. Dadecheng, Hengyu, Qingyu, Yuanyi, etc., advanced to over 5 yuan. Dingkang, Yuanmao Yong supplied on the high, and Huabi sold November shillings at 6.875, and it retreated to 1.5 yuan. Afterwards, the market atmosphere was still sharp. After Hengyu, Fuxing Yong, Dadecheng advanced, the price was raised to 8 yuan again. Small investors and Dadecheng, Zhaofeng, Changqing, Fayong, Fuxing, Hengyu, etc., suddenly came to sell off. The banks also filled shillings at 6.875, and the price broke the 1,000 yuan mark, retreating to 999 yuan. Hengxing Yuan and Fuxing Yong came in on the dip, and the price rose to 1,006 yuan again. Afterwards, Hengxing, Dadecheng, Yuanmao Yong, Shengsheng Dafu, Yu Qingyong, etc., sold off together. Unfavorable rumors spread. The current US dollar price of 32.5 yuan has been sold from Korea. Thereafter, there were few buyers for 5.625, and the 1,000 yuan mark was broken first. Selling pressure increased, and the price fell to 990 yuan. Qingyu, Fu Changheng, Yujin to 4.5 yuan, but Huabi came out, shillings in January already at 875, Yuan Mao Yong Hongli sold to one and a half yuan, Pangen filled, American gold in December at 8125, Dadecheng and Yong Li still, and the price rose to 4.5 yuan. Afterwards, British gold was one shilling and four pence, and US currency could be settled at 33.0625 yuan. Fu Changyuan, Changyong, Qian Changxiang, Dafa, Yongxiang He, etc., sold off sharply, and the price fell to 88 yuan. Dadecheng, Shunmao, Daxing Yong bought off, and the price rose to 91.5 yuan. Yuanchun, Yuanchang, Yongtai, Fuxing Yong sold to 88 yuan again. Buyers poured in at the dip, and the market price was able to be maintained. Huixiang, Yuanchun, Shunli, Shunmao, etc., bought one after another. Even though Yuanmao Yong and Fuxing Yong supplied, they were still able to gradually pull the price up. At noon, the market closed at 994.8 yuan.

As the foreign exchange market hardened, Qian Changxiang and Dadecheng resold and the price fell to 78.5 yuan. Fuxing Yong, Dakang Fuyu, Shunli Qian Changxiang, Dadecheng, etc., bought continuously, gradually rising. The price then rose to 90.05 yuan. Meifeng filled February American gold at 4375, and Fuxing Yong, Hengyu, Dalian Gang, etc., sold off, falling to 75 yuan. Dadecheng, etc., bought off, and the price rose to 7 yuan. Yuanmao Yong came to sell and the price fell again. When the market closed, the price was 986 yuan. After the market closed, Futai Heng and Fuxing Yong, etc., bought slightly, and the price gradually rose to around 8 yuan. It was found that the highest price during the day was 1,008 yuan and the lowest price was 978.5 yuan, a difference of 29.5 yuan. As a result, the closing price fell by 31 yuan compared to the previous close.

The closing price, based on the standard speculative premium price quoted by the Central Bank, was reduced to 985.5 yuan. In terms of the closing price, it was still slightly raised, but it was raised 28 yuan less than the previous closing price. The old standard for November, because the HSBC Bank's US currency quoted price did not change, was still calculated at 31.875, which corresponded to a speculative premium price of 1,085 yuan.
